Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1201 Title.
---------------------------------------
This part is known as the "Postretirement Reemployment Restrictions Act."

Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1202 Definitions.
---------------------------------------------
As used in this part:Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1202(1): (1)(a)
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1202(1)(a): "Affiliated emergency services worker" means a person who:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1202(1)(a)(i): is employed by a participating employer;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1202(1)(a)(ii): performs emergency services for another participating employer that is a different agency;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1202(1)(a)(iii): is trained in techniques and skills required for the emergency service;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1202(1)(a)(iv): continues to receive regular training required for the service;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1202(1)(a)(v): is on the rolls as a trained affiliated emergency services worker of the participating employer; and
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1202(1)(a)(vi): provides ongoing service for a participating employer, which service may include service as a volunteer firefighter, reserve law enforcement officer, search and rescue worker, emergency medical technician, ambulance worker, park ranger, or public utilities worker.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1202(1)(b): (1)(a) "Affiliated emergency services worker" does not include a person who performs work or service but does not meet the requirements of Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1202(2): 49-11-102 "Amortization rate" means the amortization rate, as defined in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1202(3): "Part-time appointed or elected board member" means an individual who:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1202(3)(a): serves in a position:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1202(3)(a)(i): as a member of a board, commission, council, committee, panel, or other body of a participating employer; and
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1202(3)(a)(ii): that is designated in the participating employer's governing statute, charter, creation document, or similar document;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1202(3)(b): is appointed or elected to the position for a definite and fixed term of office by official and duly recorded action of the participating employer;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1202(3)(c): except for the service in the position, does not perform other work or service for compensation for the participating employer, whether as an employee or under a contract; and
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1202(3)(d): retires from a participating employer that is different than the participating employer with the position in which the person serves.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1202(4): 
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1202(4)(a): "Reemployed," "reemploy," or "reemployment" means work or service performed for a participating employer after retirement, in exchange for compensation.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1202(4)(b): Reemployment includes work or service performed on a contract for a participating employer if the retiree is:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1202(4)(b)(i): listed as the contractor; or
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1202(4)(b)(ii): an owner, partner, or principal of the contractor.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1202(5): (5)(b)(i)(A); 49-11-621; Title 49, Chapter 11, Part 13, Phased Retirement "Retiree":

Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1202(5)(a)(i): retired from a participating employer; and
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1202(5)(a)(ii): begins reemployment on or after July 1, 2010, with a participating employer; and
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1202(5)(b): (5)(b)(i)(A); 49-11-621; Title 49, Chapter 11, Part 13, Phased Retirement does not include a person:

Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1203(1)(a): This part does not apply to employment as an elected official if the elected official's position is not full time as certified by the participating employer.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1203(1)(b): The provisions of this part apply to an elected official whose elected position is full time as certified by the participating employer.

Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1203(2)(b)(i): 63A-3-106 Section

Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1203(3): This part does not apply to a person who is reemployed as an active senior judge or an active senior justice court judge as described by Utah State Court Rules, appointed to hear cases by the Utah Supreme Court in accordance with Article VIII, Section 4, Utah Constitution.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1203(4): An exemption under this section from the provisions of this part is available only for a member who, at the time of retirement, is at least:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1203(4)(a): 50 years old, if the member is retiring from a public safety system or firefighter retirement system; or
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1203(4)(b): 55 years old.

Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1204(3)(b): continue to receive the retiree's retirement allowance, forfeit earning additional service credit, and forfeit any retirement-related contribution from the participating employer that reemployed the retiree.

Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1204 General restrictions -- Election following one-year separation -- Amortization rate.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1204(1): A retiree may not for the same period of reemployment:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1204(1)(a): 
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1204(1)(a)(i): earn additional service credit; or
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1204(1)(a)(ii): receive any retirement related contribution from a participating employer; and
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1204(1)(b): receive a retirement allowance.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1204(2): 49-11-1205
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1204(2)(a): 49-11-1205 Except as provided under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1204(2)(b): If the office cancels the retiree's retirement allowance under Subsection (2)(a), the retiree may be eligible to earn additional service credit in the reemployed position and receive an allowance in accordance with Subsections (4)(a) and (5) and other provisions of this title.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1204(3): If a reemployed retiree, in accordance with Subsection (2)(a), is exempt from having the allowance cancelled, including for completing the one-year separation from employment with a participating employer, the retiree may elect to:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1204(3)(a): cancel the retiree's retirement allowance and instead earn additional service credit in the reemployed position and receive an allowance in accordance with Subsections (4)(a) and (5) and other provisions of this title; or
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1204(3)(b): continue to receive the retiree's retirement allowance, not earn additional service credit, and not receive any retirement-related contribution from the participating employer that reemployed the retiree.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1204(4): 49-11-1205
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1204(4)(a): If a retiree's retirement allowance is cancelled and the retiree is eligible for retirement coverage in a reemployed position, the office shall reinstate the retiree to active member status on the first day of the month following the date of the employee's eligible reemployment.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1204(4)(b): Except as provided under Subsection (4)(c), if the retiree is not otherwise eligible for retirement coverage in the reemployed position, the participating employer that reemploys the retiree shall contribute the amortization rate to the office on behalf of the retiree.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1204(4)(c): 49-11-1205 A participating employer that reemploys a retiree in accordance with Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1204(5): 
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1204(5)(a): For a retiree reinstated to active member status under Subsection (4)(a) who retires within two years from the date of reemployment, the office:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1204(5)(a)(i): may not recalculate a retirement benefit for the retiree; and
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1204(5)(a)(ii): shall resume the allowance that was being paid to the retiree at the time of the cancellation.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1204(5)(b): Subject to Subsection (1), for a retiree who is reinstated to active membership under Subsection (4)(a) and retires two or more years after the date of reinstatement to active membership, the office shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1204(5)(b)(i): resume the allowance that was being paid at the time of cancellation; and
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1204(5)(b)(ii): calculate an additional allowance for the retiree based on the formula in effect at the date of the subsequent retirement for all service credit accrued between the first and subsequent retirement dates.

Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1205 Postretirement reemployment restriction exceptions.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1205(1): 78A-11-102
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1205(1)(a): 78A-11-102 The office may not cancel the retirement allowance of a retiree who is reemployed with a participating employer within one year of the retiree's retirement date if:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1205(1)(a)(i): the retiree is not reemployed by a participating employer for a period of at least 60 days from the retiree's retirement date;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1205(1)(a)(ii): the retiree has a bona fide termination of employment on the retiree's retirement date;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1205(1)(a)(iii): upon reemployment after the break in service under Subsection (1)(a)(i), the retiree does not receive any employer paid benefits, including:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1205(1)(a)(iii)(A): retirement service credit or retirement-related contributions;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1205(1)(a)(iii)(B): medical benefits;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1205(1)(a)(iii)(C): dental benefits;

Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1205(1)(a)(iii)(E): paid time off, including sick, annual, or other type of leave; and
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1205(1)(a)(iv): 78A-11-102
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1205(1)(a)(iv)(A): the retiree does not earn in any calendar year of reemployment an amount in excess of the lesser of $15,000 or one-half of the retiree's final average salary upon which the retiree's retirement allowance is based; or

Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1205(2)(a)(iii): had less than 30 years of service credit but had sufficient service credit to retire, with an unreduced allowance making the public safety service employee ineligible for long-term disability payments under Chapter 21, Public Employees' Long-Term Disability Act, or a substantially similar long-term disability program;

Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1209 Reporting requirement.

Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1209(1)(b): the number of retirees described in Subsection (1)(a) who are public employee retirees and the number who are public safety or firefighter retirees;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1209(1)(c): the average number of years of service credit before retirement for each type of retiree; and
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1209(1)(d): the number of retirees who reemployed on or after July 1, 2025, and have subsequently retired.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1209(2): 49-11-1204; 49-11-1205 The office shall report the information described in Subsection (1) separately for retirees who reemploy under Section


Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1301 Definitions.
---------------------------------------------
As used in this part:Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1301(1): 49-11-102 "Amortization rate" means the amortization rate, as defined in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1301(2): "Full-time" means a:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1301(2)(a): regular full-time employee whose term of employment for a participating employer contemplates continued employment during a fiscal or calendar year and whose employment normally requires an average of 40 hours or more per week and who receives benefits normally provided by the participating employer;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1301(2)(b): teacher whose term of employment for a participating employer contemplates continued employment during a school year and who teaches full time;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1301(2)(c): firefighter service employee whose employment normally requires an average of 2,080 hours of regularly scheduled firefighter service per year; and
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1301(2)(d): public safety service employee whose employment normally requires an average of 2,080 hours of regularly scheduled public safety service per year.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1301(3): "Half-time" means:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1301(3)(a): a regular employee whose term of employment for a participating employer contemplates continued employment during a fiscal or calendar year and whose employment normally requires an average of 20 hours per week and who receives benefits normally provided by the participating employer;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1301(3)(b): a teacher whose term of employment for a participating employer contemplates continued employment during a school year and who teaches half time;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1301(3)(c): a firefighter service employee whose employment normally requires an average of 1,040 hours of regularly scheduled firefighter service per year;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1301(3)(d): a public safety service employee whose employment normally requires an average of 1,040 hours of regularly scheduled public safety service per year; and
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1301(3)(e): for a retiree employed before retirement as a public safety service employee or a firefighter service employee in a position for which the participating employer established a regularly scheduled work period in excess of 2,080 hours per year, one-half of that regularly scheduled work period as long as the retiree has continuing employment in that same position.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1301(4): "Phased retirement" means continuing employment:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1301(4)(a): on a half-time basis of a retiree with the same participating employer following the retiree's retirement date while the retiree receives a reduced retirement allowance; or
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1301(4)(b): on a three-quarter time basis of a retiree with the same participating employer following the retiree's retirement date while the retiree receives a reduced retirement allowance if the retiree is employed as a public safety service employee or a firefighter service employee.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1301(5): "Three-quarter time" means:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1301(5)(a): a firefighter service employee whose employment normally requires an average of 1,560 hours of regularly scheduled firefighter service per year;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1301(5)(b): a public safety service employee whose employment normally requires an average of 1,560 hours of regularly scheduled public safety service per year; and
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1301(5)(c): for a retiree who was employed before retirement as a public safety service employee or a firefighter service employee in a position for which the participating employer established a regularly scheduled work period in excess of 2,080 hours per year, three quarters of that regularly scheduled work period as long as the retiree has continuing employment in that same position.

Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1303(3): (4) Except as provided in Subsection

Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1303(3)(b): the participating employer employs the retiree on a half-time basis;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1303(3)(c): a participating employer that employs the retiree shall contribute the amortization rate to the office;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1303(3)(d): the retiree or an alternate payee may not receive an annual cost-of-living adjustment to the retiree's or alternate payee's allowance;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1303(3)(e): any death benefits payable to a surviving spouse or other beneficiary shall be paid based on 100% of the retiree's retirement allowance;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1303(3)(f): the retiree may not receive any employer provided retirement benefits, service credit accruals, or any retirement related contributions from the participating employer; and

Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1303(4)(b): For the period of the phased retirement:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1303(4)(b)(i): the retiree is employed as a public safety service employee or a firefighter service employee;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1303(4)(b)(ii): the retiree receives 25% of the retiree's monthly allowance;

Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1303(4)(b)(iv): a participating employer that employs the retiree shall contribute to the office the certified contribution rate applicable to the system that would have covered the retiree if the retiree's part-time position were considered to be an eligible, full-time position within the system;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1303(4)(b)(v): the retiree or an alternate payee may not receive an annual cost-of-living adjustment to the retiree's or alternate payee's allowance;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1303(4)(b)(vi): any death benefits payable to a surviving spouse or other beneficiary shall be paid based on 100% of the retiree's retirement allowance;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1303(4)(b)(vii): the retiree may not receive any employer provided retirement benefits, service credit accruals, or any retirement related contributions from the participating employer; and

Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1304 Phased retirement agreements.
--------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1304(1): The participating employer and a willing and eligible retiree shall enter into a written agreement to participate in phased retirement.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1304(2): The agreement shall specify the period of the phased retirement and, at the discretion of the agreeing parties, address:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1304(2)(a): hours of work;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1304(2)(b): job duties; and
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1304(2)(c): other arrangements related to the employment.

Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1307 Phased retirement -- Adjustments or termination.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1307(1): The Legislature may make adjustments to or terminate the phased retirement option created under this part, including:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1307(1)(a): amending phased retirement eligibility, restrictions, scope, or duration provisions;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1307(1)(b): closing phased retirement to additional retirees; or
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1307(1)(c): terminating phased retirement for all participating retirees.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1307(2): A participating employer and retiree enter into a phased retirement agreement subject to the adjustments or termination reserved in this section.


Utah Code Annotated § 49-11-1308 Rulemaking.
--------------------------------------------
The board may make rules to implement this part.

Utah Code Annotated - Title 49 - Chapter 12 - Public Employees' Contributory Retirement Act
*******************************************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-101 Title.
--------------------------------------
This chapter is known as the "Public Employees' Contributory Retirement Act."

Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-102 Definitions.
--------------------------------------------
As used in this chapter:Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-102(1): (1)(b)(i); (ii); (iii); (iv)
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-102(1)(a): "Benefits normally provided" means a benefit offered by an employer, including:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-102(1)(a)(i): a leave benefit of any kind;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-102(1)(a)(ii): insurance coverage of any kind if the employer pays some or all of the premium for the coverage;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-102(1)(a)(iii): employer contributions to a health savings account, health reimbursement account, health reimbursement arrangement, or medical expense reimbursement plan; and
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-102(1)(a)(iv): a retirement benefit of any kind if the employer pays some or all of the cost of the benefit.

Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-103 Creation of system.
---------------------------------------------------
There is created for members employed by a participating employer the "Public Employees' Contributory Retirement System."

Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-104 Creation of trust fund.
-------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-104(1): There is created the "Public Employees' Contributory Retirement Trust Fund" for the purpose of paying the benefits and costs of administering this system.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-104(2): The fund shall consist of all money paid into it, including interest, in accordance with this chapter, whether in the form of cash, securities, or other assets, and of all money received from any other source.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-104(3): Chapter 11, Utah State Retirement Systems Administration Custody, management, and investment of the fund shall be governed by

Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-204 Higher education employees' eligibility requirements -- Election between different retirement plans -- Classification requirements -- Transfer between systems -- One-time election window -- Rulemaking.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-204(1): 
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-204(1)(a): A regular full-time employee of an institution of higher education who is eligible to participate in either this system or a public or private retirement system, organization, or company, designated as described in Subsection (1)(c), shall, not later than January 1, 1979, elect to participate exclusively in this system or in an annuity contract allowed under this Subsection (1).
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-204(1)(b): The election is final, and no right exists to make any further election.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-204(1)(c): The Utah Board of Higher Education shall designate the public or private retirement systems, organizations, or companies that a regular full-time employee of an institution of higher education is eligible to participate in under Subsection (1)(a).
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-204(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-204(2)(a): Except as provided under Subsection (2)(c), a regular full-time employee hired by an institution of higher education after January 1, 1979, may participate only in the retirement plan which attaches to the person's employment classification.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-204(2)(b): Each institution of higher education shall prepare or amend existing employment classifications, under the direction of the Utah Board of Higher Education, so that each classification is assigned with either:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-204(2)(b)(i): this system; or
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-204(2)(b)(ii): a public or private system, organization, or company designated by the Utah Board of Higher Education.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-204(2)(c): Notwithstanding a person's employment classification assignment under Subsection (2)(b), a regular full-time employee who begins employment with an institution of higher education on or after May 11, 2010, has a one-time irrevocable election to continue participation in this system, if the employee has service credit in this system before the date of employment.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-204(3): Notwithstanding an employment classification assignment change made under Subsection (2)(b), a regular full-time employee hired by an institution of higher education after January 1, 1979, whose employment classification requires participation in this system may elect to continue participation in this system.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-204(4): A regular full-time employee hired by an institution of higher education after January 1, 1979, whose employment classification requires participation in this system shall participate in this system.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-204(5):

Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-301 Contributions -- Two levels -- Election by a participating employer to pay employee contributions -- Accounting for and vesting of member contributions -- Deductions.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-301(1): Participating employers and members shall jointly pay the certified contribution rates to the office to maintain this system on a financially and actuarially sound basis.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-301(2): For purposes of determining contribution rates, this system is divided into two levels according to participating employers as follows:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-301(2)(a): Level A includes the state, its independent agencies, independent entities, public corporations, and other instrumentalities, all participating educational institutions, and all other participating employers whose activities are associated with participating educational institutions.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-301(2)(b): Level B includes all other participating employers in this system.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-301(3): 
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-301(3)(a): A participating employer may elect to pay all or part of the required member contributions, in addition to the required participating employer contributions.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-301(3)(b): Any amount contributed by a participating employer under this section shall vest to the member's benefit as though the member had made the contribution.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-301(3)(c): The required member contributions shall be reduced by the amount that is paid by the participating employer.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-301(4): 
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-301(4)(a): All member contributions are credited by the office to the account of the individual member.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-301(4)(b): This amount, together with refund interest, is held in trust for the payment of benefits to the member or the member's beneficiaries.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-301(4)(c): All member contributions are vested and nonforfeitable.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-301(5): 
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-301(5)(a): Each member is considered to consent to payroll deductions of member contributions.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-301(5)(b): The payment of compensation less these payroll deductions is considered full payment for services rendered by the member.

Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-402 Service retirement plans -- Calculation of retirement allowance.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-402(1): 49-12-701
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-402(1)(a): 49-12-701 Except as provided under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-402(1)(b): Options Two, Three, Four, Five, and Six are modifications of the Option One calculation.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-402(2): The Option One benefit is an annual allowance calculated as follows:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-402(2)(a): If the retiree is at least 65 years of age or has accrued at least 30 years of service credit, the allowance is:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-402(2)(a)(i): an amount equal to 1.25% of the retiree's final average monthly salary multiplied by the number of years of service credit accrued prior to July 1, 1975; plus
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-402(2)(a)(ii): an amount equal to 2% of the retiree's final average monthly salary multiplied by the number of years of service credit accrued on and after July 1, 1975.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-402(2)(b): If the retiree is less than 65 years of age, the allowance shall be reduced 3% for each year of retirement from age 60 to age 65, unless the member has 30 or more years of accrued credit in which event no reduction is made to the allowance.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-402(2)(c): 
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-402(2)(c)(i): Years of service includes any fractions of years of service to which the retiree may be entitled.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-402(2)(c)(ii): At the time of retirement, if a retiree's combined years of actual, not purchased, service credit is within 1/10 of one year of the total years of service credit required for retirement, the retiree shall be considered to have the total years of service credit required for retirement.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-402(2)(d): An Option One allowance is only payable to the member during the member's lifetime.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-402(3): 49-11-609; 49-11-610 The allowance payable under Options Two, Three, Four, Five, and Six is calculated by reducing an Option One benefit based on actuarial computations to provide the following:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-402(3)(a): 49-11-609; 49-11-610 Option Two is a reduced allowance paid to and throughout the lifetime of the retiree, and, if the retiree receives less in annuity payments than the amount of the retiree's member contributions, the remaining balance of the retiree's member contributions shall be paid in accordance with Sections
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-402(3)(b): Option Three is a reduced allowance paid to and throughout the lifetime of the retiree, and, upon the death of the retiree, the same reduced allowance paid to and throughout the lifetime of the retiree's lawful spouse at the time of retirement.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-402(3)(c): Option Four is a reduced allowance paid to and throughout the lifetime of the retiree, and upon the death of the retiree, an amount equal to 1/2 of the retiree's allowance paid to and throughout the lifetime of the retiree's lawful spouse at the time of retirement.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-402(3)(d): Option Five is a modification of Option Three so that if the lawful spouse at the time of retirement predeceases the retiree, an allowance equivalent to the amount payable at the time of initial retirement under Option One shall be paid to the retiree for the remainder of the retiree's life, beginning on the first day of the month following the month in which the:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-402(3)(d)(i): spouse died, if notification and supporting documentation for the death are received by the office within 90 days of the spouse's death; or
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-402(3)(d)(ii): notification and supporting documentation for the death are received by the office, if the notification and supporting documentation are received by the office more than 90 days after the spouse's death.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-402(3)(e): Option Six is a modification of Option Four so that if the lawful spouse at the time of retirement predeceases the retiree, an allowance equivalent to the amount payable at the time of initial retirement under Option One shall be paid to the retiree for the remainder of the retiree's life, beginning on the first day of the month following the month in which the:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-402(3)(e)(i): spouse died, if notification and supporting documentation for the death are received by the office within 90 days of the spouse's death; or
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-402(3)(e)(ii): notification and supporting documentation for the death are received by the office, if the notification and supporting documentation are received by the office more than 90 days after the spouse's death.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-402(4): 49-12-203(1)(b)
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-402(4)(a): 
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-402(4)(a)(i): The final average salary is limited in the computation of that part of an allowance based on service rendered prior to July 1, 1967, during a period when the retiree received employer contributions on a portion of compensation from an educational institution toward the payment of the premium required on a retirement annuity contract with a public or private system, organization, or company designated by the Utah Board of Higher Education to $4,800.

Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-403 Allowance payable by lump sum payment.
----------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-403(1): If a retiree's allowance, as computed under this chapter, amounts to $25 or less, the allowance may be settled by the office by making a lump-sum payment of an amount actuarially equivalent to the allowance.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-403(2): A payment made under this section constitutes a full and complete settlement of the retiree's claim against this system.

Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-407 Annual cost-of-living adjustment.
-----------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-407(1): 49-12-402; 49-12-404 The office shall make an annual cost-of-living adjustment to:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-407(1)(a): 49-12-402; 49-12-404 an original allowance paid under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-407(1)(b): an original payment made to an alternate payee under a domestic relations order, if the payment is to be paid as a percentage of the allowance rather than a specific dollar amount.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-407(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-407(2)(a): The original allowance shall be increased by the annual increase in the Consumer Price Index up to a maximum of 4%.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-407(2)(b): Annual increases in the Consumer Price Index in excess of 4% shall be  accumulated and used in subsequent adjustments when the annual increase in the Consumer Price Index is less than 4%.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-407(3): The Consumer Price Index used in calculating adjustments shall be a United States Bureau of Labor Statistics Consumer Price Index average as determined by the board.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-407(4): The cost-of-living adjustment made under this section may not decrease the allowance.

Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-409 Purchase of service credit -- Conditions -- Cost -- Nondiscrimination policy.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-409(1): 
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-409(1)(a): A member may purchase or a member and a participating employer may jointly purchase a maximum of five years of service credit which cannot otherwise be purchased under this title.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-409(1)(b): At a minimum, the years of service credit purchased shall be sufficient to allow the member to meet the retirement eligibility requirements of this system with no actuarial reduction.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-409(1)(c): The member's retirement date shall be immediately after the purchase of years of service credit.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-409(1)(d): The member shall pay at least 5% of the cost of the purchase.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-409(1)(e): To qualify for a purchase of service credit under this section, the member shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-409(1)(e)(i): have at least five years of service credit; and
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-409(1)(e)(ii): otherwise meet federal eligibility requirements.

Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-409(3): Prior to making any purchase of years of service credit under this section, a participating employer shall adopt a purchase policy that includes nondiscriminatory participation standards for all regular full-time employees.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-409(4): Only members retiring from this system may purchase service credit under this section.

Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-501(12): A death benefit under this section may not be paid to a beneficiary of a retiree under this system.


Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-601 Disability retirement -- Medical examinations -- Reemployment of retirant with a disability -- Cancellation of benefit -- Service credit -- Retirant with a disability engaging in gainful employment -- Reduction of allowance -- Refusal to submit to medical examination.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-601(1): Only members of this system who became eligible for a disability retirement allowance before January 1, 1983, are covered under this section.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-601(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-601(2)(a): The board may, upon the recommendation of the administrator, require any retirant who has been retired for disability and who has not attained the age of 60 years, to undergo a medical examination by a physician, physician assistant, or surgeon, appointed by the board, at the place of residence of the retirant or other place mutually agreed upon.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-601(2)(b): Upon the basis of the examination, the board shall determine whether the retirant with a disability is still incapacitated, physically or mentally, for service under this chapter.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-601(2)(c): If the board determines that the retirant is not incapacitated, the retirement allowance shall be cancelled and the retirant shall be reinstated immediately to a position of the same class as that held by the retirant when retired for disability.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-601(2)(d): If any employing unit is unable to reinstate the retirant, the board shall continue the disability retirement allowance of the retirant until employment is available.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-601(3): 
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-601(3)(a): If a retirant with a disability under this system reenters covered service and is eligible for membership in the retirement system, the retirement allowance shall be cancelled and the retirant shall immediately become a member of the retirement system.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-601(3)(b): 
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-601(3)(b)(i): The member's individual account shall be credited with an amount which is the actuarial equivalent, at the time of reentry, based on a disabled life, of that portion of the member's retirement allowance which was derived from the member's accumulated contributions.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-601(3)(b)(ii): The amount credited may not exceed the amount of accumulated contributions standing at the time of retirement.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-601(3)(c): Each member shall receive credit for the service in the member's account at the time of retirement.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-601(4): (6) If the retirement allowance of any retirant with a disability is cancelled for any cause other than reentry into service, the retirant shall be paid the accumulated contributions less the amounts prescribed by Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-601(5): (5)
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-601(5)(a): If any member retired for disability engages in a gainful occupation prior to attaining age 60, the administrator shall reduce the amount of the retirement allowance to an amount which, when added to the compensation earned monthly by the retirant in that occupation, may not exceed the amount of the final average monthly salary on the basis of which the current service retirement allowance was determined.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-601(5)(b): (5) If the earning capacity of the retirant is further altered, the administrator may further alter the retirement allowance as provided in this Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-601(5)(c): In no event, however, may the retirement benefit be reduced below that portion of the retirant's allowance derived from the retirant's own accumulated contributions.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-601(5)(d): When the retirant reaches age 60, the retirement allowance shall be made equal to the amount upon which the retirant was originally retired and may not again be modified for any cause.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-601(6): 
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-601(6)(a): If any member who retired for disability under age 60, refuses to submit to a medical examination, the retirement allowance may be discontinued until the retirant withdraws that refusal.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-601(6)(b): If the refusal continues for one year the disability status may be cancelled and membership terminated.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-601(6)(c): 
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-601(6)(c)(i): The retirant's accumulated contribution account shall be the actuarial equivalent on the date of the retirant's change of status, based on a disabled life, of that portion of the disability retirement allowance which was derived from the retirant's accumulated contributions.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-12-601(6)(c)(ii): The amount credited may not exceed the amount of the retirant's accumulated contributions at the time of disability retirement.

Utah Code Annotated - Title 49 - Chapter 13 - Public Employees' Noncontributory Retirement Act
**********************************************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-101 Title.
--------------------------------------
This chapter is known as the "Public Employees' Noncontributory Retirement Act."

Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-102 Definitions.
--------------------------------------------
As used in this chapter:Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-102(1): 49-12-102 "Benefits normally provided" means the same as that term is defined in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-102(2): 53F-2-513; (2)
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-102(2)(a): "Compensation" means the total amount of payments made by a participating employer to a member of this system for services rendered to the participating employer, including:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-102(2)(a)(i): bonuses;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-102(2)(a)(ii): cost-of-living adjustments;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-102(2)(a)(iii): other payments currently includable in gross income and that are subject to social security deductions, including any payments in excess of the maximum amount subject to deduction under social security law; and
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-102(2)(a)(iv): amounts that the member authorizes to be deducted or reduced for salary deferral or other benefits authorized by federal law.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-102(2)(b): "Compensation" for purposes of this chapter may not exceed the amount allowed under Internal Revenue Code, Section 401(a)(17).
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-102(2)(c): 53F-2-513 "Compensation" does not include:

Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-102(2)(c)(iii): compensation paid to a temporary employee, an exempt employee, or an employee otherwise ineligible for service credit;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-102(2)(c)(iv): any payments upon termination, including accumulated vacation, sick leave payments, severance payments, compensatory time payments, or any other special payments;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-102(2)(c)(v): any allowances or payments to a member for costs or expenses paid by the participating employer, including automobile costs, uniform costs, travel costs, tuition costs, housing costs, insurance costs, equipment costs, and dependent care costs; or

Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-103 Creation of system.
---------------------------------------------------
There is created for members employed by a participating employer the "Public Employees' Noncontributory Retirement System."

Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-104 Creation of trust fund.
-------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-104(1): There is created the "Public Employees' Noncontributory Retirement Trust Fund" for the purpose of paying the benefits and costs of administering this system.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-104(2): The fund shall consist of all money paid into it, including interest, in accordance with this chapter, whether in the form of cash, securities, or other assets, and of all money received from any other source.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-104(3): Chapter 11, Utah State Retirement Systems Administration Custody, management, and investment of the fund shall be governed by

Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-204 Higher education employees' eligibility requirements -- Election between different retirement plans -- Classification requirements -- Transfer between systems -- One-time election window -- Rulemaking.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-204(1): 
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-204(1)(a): A regular full-time employee of an institution of higher education who is eligible to participate in either this system or in a retirement system with a public or private retirement system, organization, or company, designated as described in Subsection (1)(c), shall, not later than January 1, 1979, elect to participate exclusively in this system or in an annuity contract allowed under this Subsection (1)(a).
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-204(1)(b): The election is final, and no right exists to make any further election.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-204(1)(c): The Utah Board of Higher Education shall designate the public or private retirement systems, organizations, or companies that a regular full-time employee of an institution of higher education is eligible to participate in under Subsection (1)(a).
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-204(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-204(2)(a): Except as provided under Subsection (2)(c), a regular full-time employee hired by an institution of higher education after January 1, 1979, may participate only in the retirement plan which attaches to the person's employment classification.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-204(2)(b): Each institution of higher education shall prepare or amend existing employment classifications, under the direction of the Utah Board of Higher Education, so that each classification is assigned with either:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-204(2)(b)(i): this system; or
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-204(2)(b)(ii): a public or private system, organization, or company designated by except as provided in Subsection (2)(b)(ii)(B), the Utah Board of Higher Education.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-204(2)(c): Notwithstanding a person's employment classification assignment under Subsection (2)(b), a regular full-time employee who begins employment with an institution of higher education on or after May 11, 2010, has a one-time irrevocable election to continue participation in this system, if the employee has service credit in this system before the date of employment.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-204(3): Notwithstanding an employment classification assignment change made under Subsection (2)(b), a regular full-time employee hired by an institution of higher education after January 1, 1979, whose employment classification requires participation in this system may elect to continue participation in this system.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-204(4): A regular full-time employee hired by an institution of higher education after January 1, 1979, whose employment classification requires participation in this system shall participate in this system.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-204(5): 
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-204(5)(a): Notwithstanding any other provision of this section, a regular full-time employee of an institution of higher education whose employment classification assignment under Subsection (2)(b) required participation in a retirement program other than this system shall have a one-time irrevocable election to participate in this system.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-204(5)(b): The election under Subsection (5)(a) shall be made before June 30, 2010.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-204(5)(c): All forms required by the office must be completed and received by the office no later than June 30, 2010, for the election to participate in this system to be effective.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-204(5)(d): Beginning July 1, 2010, a regular full-time employee of an institution of higher education who elects to be covered by this system under Subsection (5)(a) may begin to accrue service credit in this system.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-204(6): 49-11-403 A regular full-time employee of an institution of higher education who elects to be covered by this system under Subsection (2)(c) or (5)(a) may purchase periods of employment while covered under another retirement program by complying with the requirements of Section

Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-301 Contributions -- Two levels.
------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-301(1): Participating employers shall pay the certified contribution rates to the office to maintain this system on a financially and actuarially sound basis.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-301(2): For purposes of determining contribution rates, this system is divided into two levels according to participating employers as follows:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-301(2)(a): Level A includes the state, its independent agencies, independent entities, public corporations, and other instrumentalities, all participating educational institutions, and all other participating employers whose activities are associated with participating educational institutions.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-301(2)(b): Level B includes all other participating employers in this system.

Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-402 Service retirement plans -- Calculation of retirement allowance.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-402(1): (7); 49-13-701
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-402(1)(a): (7); 49-13-701 Except as provided under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-402(1)(b): Options Two, Three, Four, Five, and Six are modifications of the Option One calculation.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-402(2): The Option One benefit is an allowance calculated as follows:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-402(2)(a): If the retiree is at least 65 years of age or has accrued at least 30 years of service credit, the allowance is an amount equal to 2% of the retiree's final average monthly salary multiplied by the number of years of service credit accrued.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-402(2)(b): If the retiree is less than 65 years of age, the allowance shall be reduced 3% for each year of retirement from age 60 to age 65, plus a full actuarial reduction for each year of retirement prior to age 60, unless the member has 30 or more years of accrued credit, in which event no reduction is made to the allowance.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-402(2)(c): 
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-402(2)(c)(i): Years of service include any fractions of years of service to which the retiree may be entitled.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-402(2)(c)(ii): At the time of retirement, if a retiree's combined years of actual, not purchased, service credit is within 1/10 of one year of the total years of service credit required for retirement, the retiree shall be considered to have the total years of service credit required for retirement.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-402(2)(d): An Option One allowance is only payable to the member during the member's lifetime.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-402(3): 49-11-609; 49-11-610 The allowance payable under Options Two, Three, Four, Five, and Six is calculated by reducing an Option One benefit based on actuarial computations to provide the following:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-402(3)(a): 49-11-609; 49-11-610 Option Two is a reduced allowance paid to and throughout the lifetime of the retiree, and, if the retiree receives less in annuity payments than the amount of the retiree's member contributions, the remaining balance of the retiree's member contributions shall be paid in accordance with Sections
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-402(3)(b): Option Three is a reduced allowance paid to and throughout the lifetime of the retiree, and, upon the death of the retiree, the same reduced allowance paid to and throughout the lifetime of the retiree's lawful spouse at the time of retirement.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-402(3)(c): Option Four is a reduced allowance paid to and throughout the lifetime of the retiree, and upon the death of the retiree, an amount equal to one-half of the retiree's allowance paid to and throughout the lifetime of the retiree's lawful spouse at the time of retirement.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-402(3)(d): Option Five is a modification of Option Three so that if the lawful spouse at the time of retirement predeceases the retiree, an allowance equivalent to the amount payable at the time of initial retirement under Option One shall be paid to the retiree for the remainder of the retiree's life, beginning on the first day of the month following the month in which the:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-402(3)(d)(i): spouse died, if notification and supporting documentation for the death are received by the office within 90 days of the spouse's death; or
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-402(3)(d)(ii): notification and supporting documentation for the death are received by the office, if the notification and supporting documentation are received by the office more than 90 days after the spouse's death.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-402(3)(e): Option Six is a modification of Option Four so that if the lawful spouse at the time of retirement predeceases the retiree, an allowance equivalent to the amount payable at the time of initial retirement under Option One shall be paid to the retiree for the remainder of the retiree's life, beginning on the first day of the month following the month in which the:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-402(3)(e)(i): spouse died, if notification and supporting documentation for the death are received by the office within 90 days of the spouse's death; or
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-402(3)(e)(ii): notification and supporting documentation for the death are received by the office, if the notification and supporting documentation are received by the office more than 90 days after the spouse's death.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-402(4): 49-13-203(1)(b)
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-402(4)(a): 
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-402(4)(a)(i): The final average salary is limited in the computation of that part of an allowance based on service rendered prior to July 1, 1967, during a period when the retiree received employer contributions on a portion of compensation from an educational institution toward the payment of the premium required on a retirement annuity contract with a public or private system, organization, or company designated by the Utah Board of Higher Education to $4,800.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-402(4)(a)(ii): This limitation is not applicable to retirees who elected to continue in the Public Employees' Contributory Retirement System by July 1, 1967.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-402(4)(b): 49-13-203(1)(b) Periods of employment which are exempt from this system as permitted under Subsection

Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-405 Death of married members -- Service retirement benefits to surviving spouse.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-405(1): 49-13-402 As used in this section, "member's full allowance" means an Option Three allowance calculated under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-405(2): Upon the request of a deceased member's surviving spouse, the deceased member is considered to have retired under Option Three on the first day of the month following the month in which the member died if the following requirements are met:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-405(2)(a): the member has:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-405(2)(a)(i): 15 or more years of service credit;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-405(2)(a)(ii): attained age 62 with 10 or more years of service credit; or
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-405(2)(a)(iii): attained age 65 with four or more years of service credit; and
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-405(2)(b): the member dies leaving a surviving spouse.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-405(3): The surviving spouse who requests a benefit under this section shall apply in writing to the office.  The allowance shall begin on the first day of the month:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-405(3)(a): following the month in which the member died, if the application is received by the office within 90 days of the member's death; or
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-405(3)(b): following the month in which the application is received by the office, if the application is received by the office more than 90 days after the member's death.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-405(4): The allowance payable to a surviving spouse under Subsection (2) is:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-405(4)(a): if the member has 25 or more years of service credit at the time of death, the surviving spouse shall receive the member's full allowance;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-405(4)(b): if the member has between 20-24 years of service credit and is not age 60 or older at the time of death, the surviving spouse shall receive two-thirds of the member's full allowance;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-405(4)(c): if the member has between 15-19 years of service credit and is not age 62 or older at the time of death, the surviving spouse shall receive one-third of the member's full allowance; or

Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-407 Annual cost-of-living adjustment.
-----------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-407(1): 49-13-402; 49-13-405 The office shall make an annual cost-of-living adjustment to:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-407(1)(a): 49-13-402; 49-13-405 an original allowance paid under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-407(1)(b): an original payment made to an alternate payee under a domestic relations order, if the payment is to be paid as a percentage of the allowance rather than a specific dollar amount.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-407(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-407(2)(a): The original allowance shall be increased by the annual increase in the Consumer Price Index up to a maximum of 4%.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-407(2)(b): Annual increases in the Consumer Price Index in excess of 4% shall be accumulated and used in subsequent adjustments when the annual increase in the Consumer Price Index is less than 4%.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-407(3): The Consumer Price Index used in calculating adjustments shall be a United States Bureau of Labor Statistics Consumer Price Index average as determined by the board.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-407(4): The cost-of-living adjustment made under this section may not decrease the allowance.


Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-408 Purchase of service credit -- Conditions -- Cost -- Nondiscrimination policy.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-408(1): 
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-408(1)(a): A member may purchase or a member and a participating employer may jointly purchase a maximum of five years of service credit which cannot otherwise be purchased under this title.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-408(1)(b): At a minimum, the years of service credit purchased shall be sufficient to allow the member to meet the retirement eligibility requirements of this system with no actuarial reduction.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-408(1)(c): The member's retirement date shall be immediately after the purchase of years of service credit.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-408(1)(d): The member shall pay at least 5% of the cost of the purchase.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-408(1)(e): To qualify for a purchase of service credit under this section, the member shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-408(1)(e)(i): have at least five years of service credit; and
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-408(1)(e)(ii): otherwise meet federal eligibility requirements.

Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-408(3): Prior to making any purchase of years of service credit under this section, a participating employer shall adopt a purchase policy that includes nondiscriminatory participation standards for all regular full-time employees.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-13-408(4): Only members retiring from this system may purchase service credit under this section.

Utah Code Annotated - Title 49 - Chapter 14 - Public Safety Contributory Retirement Act
***************************************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 49-14-101 Title.
--------------------------------------
This chapter is known as the "Public Safety Contributory Retirement Act."

Utah Code Annotated § 49-14-102 Definitions.
--------------------------------------------
As used in this chapter:Utah Code Annotated § 49-14-102(1): 
Utah Code Annotated § 49-14-102(1)(a): "Compensation" means the total amount of payments that are includable in gross income received by a public safety service employee as base income for the regularly scheduled work period.  The participating employer shall establish the regularly scheduled work period.  Base income shall be determined prior to the deduction of member contributions or any amounts the public safety service employee authorizes to be deducted for salary deferral or other benefits authorized by federal law.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-14-102(1)(b): "Compensation" includes performance-based bonuses and cost-of-living adjustments.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-14-102(1)(c): "Compensation" does not include:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-14-102(1)(c)(i): overtime;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-14-102(1)(c)(ii): sick pay incentives;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-14-102(1)(c)(iii): retirement pay incentives;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-14-102(1)(c)(iv): the monetary value of remuneration paid in kind, including a residence, use of equipment or uniform, travel, or similar payments;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-14-102(1)(c)(v): a lump-sum payment or special payments covering accumulated leave; and
Utah Code Annotated § 49-14-102(1)(c)(vi): all contributions made by a participating employer under this system or under any other employee benefit system or plan maintained by a participating employer for the benefit of a member or participant.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-14-102(1)(d): "Compensation" for purposes of this chapter may not exceed the amount allowed under Internal Revenue Code Section 401(a)(17).
Utah Code Annotated § 49-14-102(2): 53-6-102 "Dispatcher" means the same as that term is defined in Section

Utah Code Annotated § 49-14-103 Creation of system.
---------------------------------------------------
There is created for members performing public safety service and who are employed by a participating employer the "Public Safety Contributory Retirement System."

Utah Code Annotated § 49-14-104 Creation of trust fund.
-------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-14-104(1): There is created the "Public Safety Contributory Retirement Trust Fund" for the purpose of paying the benefits and the costs of administering this system.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-14-104(2): The fund shall consist of a number of individual trust accounts created as needed to receive the money and assets transferred into them from the respective terminated systems, all money paid into them, including interest, in accordance with this chapter, whether in the form of cash, securities, or other assets, and of all money received from any other source.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-14-104(3): Chapter 11, Utah State Retirement Systems Administration Custody, management, and investment of the fund shall be governed by

Utah Code Annotated § 49-14-505 Benefits for surviving spouse under Division A or Division B.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
The surviving spouse, if eligible, shall receive a benefit computed under either Division A or Division B, whichever provides the larger benefit, but may not receive a benefit under both divisions if it would result in a duplicate benefit.

Utah Code Annotated § 49-14-506 Benefits payable upon death of active or inactive member without spouse or minor children.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
If an active or inactive member dies and at the time of death the member does not have a surviving spouse or minor children, the benefit payable to a designated beneficiary is a refund of the member's member contributions or $500, whichever is larger.

Utah Code Annotated § 49-14-507 Surviving spouse includes certain former spouses -- Benefit calculation for former spouse.

Utah Code Annotated - Title 49 - Chapter 15 - Public Safety Noncontributory Retirement Act
******************************************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 49-15-101 Title.
--------------------------------------
This chapter is known as the "Public Safety Noncontributory Retirement Act."

Utah Code Annotated § 49-15-102 Definitions.
--------------------------------------------
As used in this chapter:Utah Code Annotated § 49-15-102(1): 
Utah Code Annotated § 49-15-102(1)(a): "Compensation" means the total amount of payments that are includable in gross income received by a public safety service employee as base income for the regularly scheduled work period.  The participating employer shall establish the regularly scheduled work period.  Base income shall be determined prior to the deduction of any amounts the public safety service employee authorizes to be deducted for salary deferral or other benefits authorized by federal law.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-15-102(1)(b): "Compensation" includes performance-based bonuses and cost-of-living adjustments.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-15-102(1)(c): "Compensation" does not include:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-15-102(1)(c)(i): overtime;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-15-102(1)(c)(ii): sick pay incentives;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-15-102(1)(c)(iii): retirement pay incentives;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-15-102(1)(c)(iv): the monetary value of remuneration paid in kind, as in a residence, use of equipment or uniform, travel, or similar payments;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-15-102(1)(c)(v): a lump-sum payment or special payment covering accumulated leave; and
Utah Code Annotated § 49-15-102(1)(c)(vi): all contributions made by a participating employer under this system or under any other employee benefit system or plan maintained by a participating employer for the benefit of a member or participant.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-15-102(1)(d): "Compensation" for purposes of this chapter may not exceed the amount allowed under Internal Revenue Code Section 401(a)(17).
Utah Code Annotated § 49-15-102(2): 53-6-102 "Dispatcher" means the same as that term is defined in Section

Utah Code Annotated § 49-15-102(10): "Years of service credit" means the number of periods, each to consist of 12 full months as determined by the board, whether consecutive or not, during which a public safety service employee was employed by a participating employer, including time the public safety service employee was absent in the service of the United States government on military duty.


Utah Code Annotated § 49-15-103 Creation of system.
---------------------------------------------------
There is created for members performing public safety service and who are employed by a participating employer the "Public Safety Noncontributory Retirement System."

Utah Code Annotated § 49-15-104 Creation of trust fund.
-------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-15-104(1): There is created the "Public Safety Noncontributory Retirement Trust Fund" for the purpose of paying the benefits and the costs of administering this system.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-15-104(2): The fund shall consist of a number of individual trust accounts created as needed to receive the money and assets transferred into them from the respective terminated systems, all money paid into them, including interest, in accordance with this chapter, whether in the form of cash, securities, or other assets, and of all money received from any other source.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-15-104(3): Chapter 11, Utah State Retirement Systems Administration Custody, management, and investment of the fund shall be governed by

Utah Code Annotated § 49-15-301 Contributions -- Two divisions -- Subdivisions.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-15-301(1): Participating employers shall pay the certified contribution rates to the office to maintain this system on a financially and actuarially sound basis.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-15-301(2): For purposes of determining contribution rates, this system is divided into two divisions according to Social Security coverage:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-15-301(2)(a): members of this system with on-the-job Social Security coverage are Division A; and
Utah Code Annotated § 49-15-301(2)(b): members of this system without on-the-job Social Security coverage are in Division B.

Utah Code Annotated § 49-15-301(4): Contribution rates for a participating employer may be different than for other participating employers based on the participating employer's current funding status and actuarial experience.

Utah Code Annotated § 49-15-501 Death of active member in Division A -- Payment of benefits.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-15-501(1): 49-15-301; 49-15-402; 49-15-504; (1)(a)(ii) If an active member of this system enrolled in Division A under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 49-15-501(1)(a): 49-15-402; 49-15-504 If the death is classified by the office as a line-of-duty death, benefits are payable as follows:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-15-501(1)(a)(i): If the member has accrued less than 20 years of public safety service credit, the surviving spouse shall receive a lump sum equal to six months of the active member's final average salary and an allowance equal to 30% of the member's final average monthly salary.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-15-501(1)(a)(ii): 49-15-402; 49-15-504 If the member has accrued 20 or more years of public safety service credit, the member shall be considered to have retired with an allowance calculated under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 49-15-501(1)(b): (1)(a)(ii) If the death is not classified as a line-of-duty death by the office, benefits are payable as follows:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-15-501(1)(b)(i): If the member has accrued less than 10 years of public safety service credit, the surviving spouse shall receive the sum of $1,000 or a refund of the member's member contributions, whichever is greater.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-15-501(1)(b)(ii): If the member has accrued 10 or more years, but less than 20 years of public safety service credit at the time of death, the surviving spouse shall receive the sum of $500, plus an allowance equal to 2% of the member's final average monthly salary for each year of service credit accrued by the member up to a maximum of 30% of the member's final average monthly salary.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-15-501(1)(b)(iii): (1)(a)(ii) If the member has accrued 20 or more years of public safety service credit, the benefit shall be calculated as provided in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 49-15-501(2): (1)(b)(i) Except as provided under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 49-15-501(3): If a benefit is not distributed under this section, and the member has designated a beneficiary, the member's member contribution shall be paid to the beneficiary.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-15-501(4): 
Utah Code Annotated § 49-15-501(4)(a): A surviving spouse who requests a benefit under this section shall apply in writing to the office.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-15-501(4)(b): The allowance shall begin on the first day of the month following the month in which the:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-15-501(4)(b)(i): member died, if the application is received by the office within 90 days of the member's death; or
Utah Code Annotated § 49-15-501(4)(b)(ii): application is received by the office, if the application is received by the office more than 90 days after the member's death.

Utah Code Annotated § 49-15-505 Benefits for surviving spouse under Division A or Division B.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
The surviving spouse, if eligible, shall receive a benefit computed under either Division A or Division B, whichever provides the larger benefit, but may not receive a benefit under both divisions if it would result in a duplicate benefit.

Utah Code Annotated § 49-15-506 Benefits payable upon death of active or inactive member without spouse or minor children.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
If an active or inactive member dies and at the time of death the member does not have a surviving spouse or minor children, the benefit payable to a designated beneficiary is a refund of the member's member contributions or $500, whichever is larger.
