Utah Code Annotated - Title 49 - Chapter 16 - Firefighters' Retirement Act
**************************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-101 Title.
--------------------------------------
This chapter is known as the "Firefighters' Retirement Act."

Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-102 Definitions.
--------------------------------------------
As used in this chapter:Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-102(1): 
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-102(1)(a): "Compensation" means the total amount of payments that are includable as gross income received by a firefighter service employee as base income for the regularly scheduled work period.  The participating employer shall establish the regularly scheduled work period.  Base income shall be determined prior to the deduction of member contributions or any amounts the firefighter service employee authorizes to be deducted for salary deferral or other benefits authorized by federal law.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-102(1)(b): "Compensation" includes performance-based bonuses and cost-of-living adjustments.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-102(1)(c): "Compensation" does not include:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-102(1)(c)(i): overtime;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-102(1)(c)(ii): sick pay incentives;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-102(1)(c)(iii): retirement pay incentives;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-102(1)(c)(iv): remuneration paid in kind such as a residence, use of equipment, uniforms, travel, or similar payments;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-102(1)(c)(v): a lump-sum payment or special payments covering accumulated leave; and
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-102(1)(c)(vi): all contributions made by a participating employer under this system or under any other employee benefit system or plan maintained by a participating employer for the benefit of a member or participant.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-102(1)(d): "Compensation" for purposes of this chapter may not exceed the amount allowed under Section 401(a)(17), Internal Revenue Code.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-102(2): (2)(a)
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-102(2)(a): "Disability" means the complete inability, due to objective medical impairment, whether physical or mental, to perform firefighter service.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-102(2)(b): (2)(a) "Disability" does not include the inability to meet an employer's required standards or tests relating to fitness, physical ability, or agility that is not a result of a disability as defined under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-102(3): 53-2d-402 "Emergency medical service personnel" means an individual who:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-102(3)(a): is:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-102(3)(a)(i): a paramedic;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-102(3)(a)(ii): an advanced emergency medical services technician; or
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-102(3)(a)(iii): an emergency medical services technician;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-102(3)(b): 53-2d-402 is required to be licensed or certified under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-102(3)(c): has a primary job duty to provide emergency medical services as a first responder.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-102(4): (4)(b); (c); (d); (4)(c); (4)(b); (14)
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-102(4)(a): (4)(b); (c); (d) "Final average salary" means the amount calculated by averaging the highest three years of annual compensation preceding retirement subject to Subsections
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-102(4)(b): (4)(c) Except as provided in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-102(4)(c): (4)(b) In cases where the participating employer provides acceptable documentation to the office the limitation in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-102(4)(c)(i): the member has transferred from another agency; or
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-102(4)(c)(ii): the member has been promoted to a new position.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-102(4)(d): (14) The annual compensation used to calculate final average salary shall be based on a period, as determined by the board, consistent with the period used to determine years of service credit in accordance with Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-102(5): 53-7-103
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-102(5)(a): 53-7-103 "Firefighter service" means employment normally requiring an average of 2,080 hours of regularly scheduled employment per year rendered by a member who is:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-102(5)(a)(i): a firefighter service employee trained in firefighter techniques and assigned to a position of hazardous duty with a regularly constituted fire department;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-102(5)(a)(ii): 53-7-103 the state fire marshal appointed under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-102(5)(a)(iii): an emergency medical service personnel.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-102(5)(b): "Firefighter service" does not include secretarial staff or other similar employees.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-102(6): 
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-102(6)(a): "Firefighter service employee" means an employee of a participating employer who provides firefighter service under this chapter.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-102(6)(b): "Firefighter service employee" does not include an employee of a regularly constituted fire department who does not perform firefighter service.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-102(7): (7)(a)
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-102(7)(a): "Line-of-duty death or disability" means a death or disability resulting from:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-102(7)(a)(i): external force, violence, or disease directly resulting from firefighter service; or
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-102(7)(a)(ii): strenuous activity, including a heart attack or stroke, that occurs during strenuous training or another strenuous activity required as an act of duty as a firefighter service employee.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-102(7)(b): (7)(a) "Line-of-duty death or disability" does not include a death or disability that:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-102(7)(b)(i): occurs during an activity that is required as an act of duty as a firefighter service employee if the activity is not a strenuous activity, including an activity that is clerical, administrative, or of a nonmanual nature;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-102(7)(b)(ii): occurs during the commission of a crime committed by the employee;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-102(7)(b)(iii): occurs when the employee's intoxication or use of alcohol or drugs, whether prescribed or nonprescribed, contributes to the employee's death or disability; or
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-102(7)(b)(iv): (7)(a) occurs in a manner other than as described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-102(7)(c): "Line-of-duty death or disability" includes the death or disability of a paid firefighter resulting from heart disease, lung disease, or a respiratory tract condition if the paid firefighter has five years of firefighter service credit.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-102(8): "Objective medical impairment" means an impairment resulting from an injury or illness that is diagnosed by a physician or physician assistant and that is based on accepted objective medical tests or findings rather than subjective complaints.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-102(9): 49-16-201 "Participating employer" means an employer that meets the participation requirements of Section
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-102(10): "Regularly constituted fire department" means a fire department that employs a fire chief who performs firefighter service for at least 2,080 hours of regularly scheduled paid employment per year.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-102(11): 
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-102(11)(a): "Strenuous activity" means engagement involving a difficult, stressful, or vigorous fire suppression, rescue, hazardous material response, emergency medical service, physical law enforcement, prison security, disaster relief, or other emergency response activity.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-102(11)(b): "Strenuous activity" includes participating in a participating employer sanctioned and funded training exercise that involves difficult, stressful, or vigorous physical activity.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-102(12): "System" means the Firefighters' Retirement System created under this chapter.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-102(13): (13)(a)
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-102(13)(a): "Volunteer firefighter" means any individual who is not regularly employed as a firefighter service employee, but who:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-102(13)(a)(i): has been trained in firefighter techniques and skills;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-102(13)(a)(ii): continues to receive regular firefighter training; and

Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-103 Creation of system.
---------------------------------------------------
There is created for members performing firefighter service and who are employed by a participating employer the "Firefighters' Retirement System."

Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-104 Creation of trust fund.
-------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-104(1): There is created the "Firefighters' Retirement Trust Fund" for the purpose of paying the benefits and costs of administering this system.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-104(2): The fund shall consist of all money and assets transferred to it from any terminated system, all money paid into it, including interest, in accordance with this chapter, whether in the form of cash, securities, or other assets, and of all money received from any other source.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-104(3): Chapter 11, Utah State Retirement Systems Administration The custody, management, and investment of the fund shall be governed by

Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-301 Contributions -- Two divisions -- Election by employer to  pay employee contributions -- Accounting for and vesting of worker contributions -- Deductions.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-301(1): 49-11-901.5 In addition to the money paid to this system under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-301(2): For purposes of determining contribution rates, this system is divided into two divisions according to Social Security coverage as follows:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-301(2)(a): members of this system with on-the-job Social Security coverage are in Division A; and
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-301(2)(b): members of this system without on-the-job Social Security coverage are in Division B.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-301(3): 
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-301(3)(a): A participating employer may elect to pay all or part of the required member contributions, in addition to the required participating employer contributions.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-301(3)(b): Any amount contributed by a participating employer under this section shall vest to the member's benefit as though the member had made the contribution.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-301(3)(c): The required member contributions shall be reduced by the amount that is paid by the participating employer.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-301(4): 
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-301(4)(a): All member contributions are credited by the office to the account of the individual member.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-301(4)(b): This amount is held in trust for the payment of benefits to the member or the member's beneficiaries.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-301(4)(c): All member contributions are vested and nonforfeitable.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-301(5): 
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-301(5)(a): Each member is considered to consent to payroll deductions of member contributions.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-301(5)(b): The payment of compensation less these payroll deductions is considered to be full payment for services rendered by the member.

Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-402 Calculation of retirement allowance.
--------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-402(1): A retiree under this system shall receive an allowance equal to:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-402(1)(a): 2.5% of final average monthly salary multiplied by the number of years of service credit, limited to 20 years; plus
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-402(1)(b): 2% of final average monthly salary, multiplied by the number of years of service credit in excess of 20 years.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-402(2): The minimum allowance payable under this section is $500.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-402(3): (3)(b); (3)(a)

Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-403 Annual cost-of-living adjustment.
-----------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-403(1): 49-16-402; Part 5, Death Benefit; Part 6, Disability Benefit The office shall  make an annual cost-of-living adjustment to:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-403(1)(a): 49-16-402; Part 5, Death Benefit; Part 6, Disability Benefit an original allowance paid under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-403(1)(b): an original payment made to an alternate payee under a domestic relations order, if the payment is to be paid as a percentage of the allowance rather than a specific dollar amount.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-403(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-403(2)(a): The original allowance shall be increased by the annual increase in the Consumer Price Index up to a maximum of 4%.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-403(2)(b): Annual increases in the Consumer Price Index in excess of 4% shall be accumulated and used in subsequent adjustments when the annual increase in the Consumer Price Index is less than 4%.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-403(3): The Consumer Price Index used in calculating adjustments shall be a United States Bureau of Labor Statistics Consumer Price Index average as determined by the board.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-403(4): The cost-of-living adjustment made under this section may not decrease the allowance.

Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-503 Benefits payable upon death of inactive member.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-503(1): If an inactive member who has less than 20 years of firefighter service credit dies, the surviving spouse, or, if there is no surviving spouse, the member's minor children shall receive a refund of the member's member contributions or $500, whichever is greater.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-503(2): 49-16-402
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-503(2)(a): If an inactive member with 20 or more years of firefighter service credit dies, the surviving spouse shall receive an allowance in the amount of 50% of the amount the member would have received had retirement occurred on the first of the month following the month in which the death occurred.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-503(2)(b): 49-16-402 This allowance shall be based on years of service credit and final average monthly salary under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-503(3): 
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-503(3)(a): A surviving spouse who requests a benefit under this section shall apply in writing to the office.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-503(3)(b): The allowance shall begin on the first day of the month:

Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-503(3)(b)(ii): following the month in which the application is received by the office, if the application is received by the office more than 90 days after the member's death.


Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-504 Benefits payable upon death of retired member.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-504(1): If a retiree who retired under either Division A or Division B dies, the retiree's surviving spouse shall receive an allowance equal to 75% of the allowance that was being paid to the retiree at the time of death.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-504(2): 49-16-502(1)(c) If the retiree retired solely under Division B and dies leaving unmarried children under the age of 21 or dependent unmarried children with a mental or physical disability, the children shall qualify for a benefit as prescribed under Subsection

Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-504(3)(b): The allowance shall begin on the first day of the month following the month in which the:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-504(3)(b)(i): member or participant died, if the application is received by the office within 90 days of the date of death of the member or participant; or
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-504(3)(b)(ii): application is received by the office, if the application is received by the office more than 90 days after the date of death of the member or participant.


Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-505 Benefits for surviving spouse under Division A or Division B.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
The surviving spouse, if eligible, shall receive a benefit computed under either Division A or Division B, whichever provides the larger benefit, but may not receive a benefit under both divisions if it would result in a duplicate benefit.

Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-506 Minimum allowance for surviving spouse.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------
The minimum allowance payable to the surviving spouse who qualifies for an allowance under Section

Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-507 Benefits payable upon death of active or inactive member without a surviving spouse or minor children.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
If an active or inactive member dies and at the time of death the member does not have a surviving spouse or minor children, the benefit payable to a designated beneficiary is a refund of the member's member contributions or $500, whichever is larger.

Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-601 Disability benefit -- Nonline-of-duty disability -- Benefits -- Monthly allowance.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-601(1): 49-16-602 An active member of this system with a disability that was not incurred in the line-of-duty may apply to the office for a disability retirement benefit subject to the following provisions:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-601(1)(a): if the member has less than five years of service credit in this system, disability benefits are not payable; and
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-601(1)(b): 49-16-602 if the condition is classified by the office as a nonline-of-duty disability and if the member has five or more years of service credit in this system, the member shall be granted a disability retirement benefit subject to Section
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-601(2): The monthly disability retirement benefit is 50% of the member's final average monthly salary.


Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-601.5 Line-of-duty disability benefit -- Benefits -- Monthly allowance.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-601.5(1): An active member of this system with a disability incurred in the line-of-duty may apply to the office for a disability retirement benefit under this section.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-601.5(2): 49-16-602 If the condition is classified by the office as a line-of-duty disability, the member shall be granted a disability retirement benefit subject to Section
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-601.5(3): A paid firefighter who has five years of firefighter service credit is eligible for a line-of-duty disability benefit resulting from heart disease, lung disease, or a respiratory tract condition.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-601.5(4): A paid firefighter who receives a service connected disability benefit for more than six months due to violence or illness other than heart disease, lung disease, or respiratory tract condition, and then returns to paid firefighter service, may not be eligible for a line-of-duty disability benefit due to heart disease, lung disease, or respiratory tract condition for two years after the firefighter returned to work unless clear and convincing evidence is presented that the heart disease, lung disease, or respiratory tract condition was directly a result of firefighter service.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-601.5(5): The monthly disability retirement benefit is 50% of the member's final average salary.


Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-602 Disability retirement -- Disability allowance eligibility -- Conversion to service retirement -- Examinations -- Reemployment.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-602(1): A member of this system who applies and is qualified for disability retirement shall receive a disability retirement benefit until the earlier of:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-602(1)(a): the date the member of this system no longer has a disability;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-602(1)(b): the date the member of this system has accumulated 20 years of firefighter service credit, including years earned while the member of this system had a disability; or
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-602(1)(c): the date the member of this system has received disability retirement benefits for the following time periods:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-602(1)(c)(i): if the member is under age 60 on the date of disability, the disability retirement benefit is payable until age 65;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-602(1)(c)(ii): if the member is 60 or 61 years of age on the date of disability, the disability retirement benefit is payable for five years;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-602(1)(c)(iii): if the member is 62 or 63 years of age on the date of disability, the disability retirement benefit is payable for four years;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-602(1)(c)(iv): if the member is 64 or 65 years of age on the date of disability, the disability retirement benefit is payable for three years;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-602(1)(c)(v): if the member is 66, 67, or 68 years of age on the date of disability, the disability retirement benefit is payable for two years; and
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-602(1)(c)(vi): if the member is 69 years of age or older on the date of disability, the disability retirement benefit is payable for one year.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-602(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-602(2)(a): 
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-602(2)(a)(i): The retiree with a disability shall receive service credit in this system during the period of disability.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-602(2)(a)(ii): If the retiree with a disability is employed by a participating employer during the period of disability, the retiree with a disability may not receive service credit for that employment.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-602(2)(b): The disability retirement shall be converted to a service retirement at the time the disability retirement benefits terminate.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-602(3): The office shall approve or disapprove applications for disability retirement benefits based upon:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-602(3)(a): the evaluation and recommendations of one or more treating physicians or physician assistants along with medical records relating to the condition;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-602(3)(b): the evaluation and recommendations of one or more independent physicians or physician assistants selected by the office; and
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-602(3)(c): receipt of documentation by the office from the participating employer that the member is mentally or physically unable to perform firefighter service.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-602(4): (4)
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-602(4)(a): A retiree with a disability who receives benefits under this section shall, upon request of the executive director, submit to a medical examination by one or more physicians or physician assistants as directed by the office.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-602(4)(b): If, after an examination, the examiners report that the retiree with a disability is physically and mentally able and capable of resuming firefighter service employment, the retiree with a disability shall be reinstated by the participating employer for which the retiree with a disability last worked at the former classification and rank of the retiree with a disability, and the disability retirement benefit shall terminate.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-602(4)(c): (4) A retiree with a disability may not be required to submit to an examination under this Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-602(4)(d): A retiree with a disability who returns to firefighter service employment with a participating employer in this system shall immediately begin accruing service credit that shall be added to that service credit that has been previously accrued, including service credit while disabled.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-602(5): A retiree with a disability is not subject to medical examinations after reaching age 55.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-602(6): Refusal or neglect of a member to submit to an examination as requested by the office either before or after a decision regarding disability benefits has been made is sufficient cause for denial, suspension, or discontinuance of benefits and if the refusal or neglect continues for one year, the rights of the member or retiree with a disability to disability retirement benefits may be revoked by the office.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-602(7): (7)
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-602(7)(a): A retiree with a disability who receives benefits under this part shall file a sworn statement with the office on or before March 15 of each year for the first five years a retiree with a disability receives benefits.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-602(7)(b): The sworn statement shall indicate whether or not the retiree with a disability engaged in any employment during the preceding year and, if so, the amount of earnings received during the calendar year.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-602(7)(c): If the total amount received in one year by a retiree with a disability for disability retirement benefits and gross earnings from other employment exceeds 125% of the final average salary of the retiree with a disability, the office shall offset the disability retirement benefit paid the following year by the amount in excess of 125% of the final average salary of the retiree with a disability.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-602(7)(d): (7)
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-602(7)(d)(i): (7) If a retiree with a disability refuses or neglects to file a sworn statement as required under this Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-602(7)(d)(ii): Upon filing the statement, the payments of the retiree with a disability shall be resumed.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-602(8): The disability retirement benefit shall be improved by the annual cost-of-living increase factor applied to retirees of the system that covered the firefighter service employee at the time of disability.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-602(9): 49-16-601 A line of duty disability allowance paid on or after January 1, 2002, under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-602(10): 
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-602(10)(a): An active member of this system with five or more years of firefighter service credit shall be eligible for a line-of-duty death or disability benefit resulting from heart disease, lung disease, or respiratory tract disease.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-602(10)(b): An active member of this system who receives a line-of-duty disability benefit for more than six months due to violence or illness other than heart disease, lung disease, or respiratory tract disease, and then returns to paid firefighter service, is not eligible for a line-of-duty death or disability benefit due to those diseases for two years after the member returned to paid firefighter service unless clear and convincing evidence is presented that the heart, lung, or respiratory tract disease was directly a result of firefighter service.

Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-603 Suspension of benefit upon settlement of workers' compensation claim.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-603(1): Settlement of a claim for workers' compensation for injury or disability shall suspend disability retirement benefits granted under this part, except for the initial three months, to a member granted the benefits until workers' compensation payments terminate.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-16-603(2): If there is a lump-sum settlement of the workers' compensation claim, the office shall suspend the disability retirement benefit until the total of suspended benefits is equal to 75% of the settlement received from workers' compensation.

Utah Code Annotated - Title 49 - Chapter 17 - Judges' Contributory Retirement Act
*********************************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 49-17-101 Title.
--------------------------------------
This chapter is known as the "Judges' Contributory Retirement Act."

Utah Code Annotated § 49-17-102 Definitions.
--------------------------------------------
As used in this chapter:Utah Code Annotated § 49-17-102(1): 
Utah Code Annotated § 49-17-102(1)(a): "Compensation" means the total amount of payments which are currently includable in gross income made by a participating employer to a member of this system for services rendered to the participating employer.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-17-102(1)(b): "Compensation" includes:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-17-102(1)(b)(i): performance-based bonuses;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-17-102(1)(b)(ii): cost-of-living adjustments;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-17-102(1)(b)(iii): payments subject to Social Security deductions;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-17-102(1)(b)(iv): any payments in excess of the maximum amount subject to deduction under Social Security law;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-17-102(1)(b)(v): amounts which the member authorizes to be deducted or reduced for salary deferral or other benefits authorized by federal law; and
Utah Code Annotated § 49-17-102(1)(b)(vi): member contributions.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-17-102(1)(c): "Compensation" for purposes of this chapter may not exceed the amount allowed under Internal Revenue Code Section 401(a)(17).
Utah Code Annotated § 49-17-102(1)(d): "Compensation," does not include:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-17-102(1)(d)(i): the monetary value of remuneration paid in kind, such as a residence or use of equipment;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-17-102(1)(d)(ii): all contributions made by a participating employer under any system or plan for the benefit of a member or participant;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-17-102(1)(d)(iii): salary paid to a temporary or exempt employee;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-17-102(1)(d)(iv): payments upon termination or any other special payments including early retirement inducements; or
Utah Code Annotated § 49-17-102(1)(d)(v): uniform, travel, or similar payments.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-17-102(2): (2)(a); (b); (c); (2)(b); (2)(a) "Final average salary" means the amount calculated by averaging the highest two years of annual compensation preceding retirement, subject to Subsections
Utah Code Annotated § 49-17-102(2)(a): (2)(b) Except as provided in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 49-17-102(2)(b): (2)(a) In cases where the participating employer provides acceptable documentation to the board, the limitation in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 49-17-102(2)(b)(i): the member has transferred from another participating employer; or
Utah Code Annotated § 49-17-102(2)(b)(ii): the member has been promoted to a new position.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-17-102(2)(c): The annual compensation used to calculate final average salary shall be based on the state's fiscal year.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-17-102(3): 78A-1-101 "Judge" means a judge or justice of the courts of record as enumerated in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 49-17-102(4): "Participating employer" means the state.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-17-102(5): "System" means the Judges' Contributory Retirement System created under this chapter.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-17-102(6): "Years of service credit" means the number of periods, each to consist of 12 full months as determined by the board, whether consecutive or not, during which a judge was employed by a participating employer.


Utah Code Annotated § 49-17-103 Creation of system.
---------------------------------------------------
There is created for judges the "Judges' Contributory Retirement System."

Utah Code Annotated § 49-17-104 Creation of trust fund.
-------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-17-104(1): There is created the "Judges' Contributory Retirement Trust Fund" for the purpose of paying the benefits and costs of administering this system.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-17-104(2): The fund shall consist of all money, including interest, and assets transferred to it under any terminated system, the money paid into it under this system, whether in the form of cash, securities, or other assets, and of all money received from any other source.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-17-104(3): Chapter 11, Utah State Retirement Systems Administration Custody, management, and investment of the fund shall be governed by

Utah Code Annotated § 49-17-401 Eligibility for an allowance -- Date of retirement -- Qualifications.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-17-401(1): A member is qualified to receive an allowance when:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-17-401(1)(a): the member ceases actual work for every participating employer that employs the member before the member's retirement date and provides evidence of the termination;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-17-401(1)(b): the member has submitted to the office a retirement application form that states the member's proposed retirement date; and
Utah Code Annotated § 49-17-401(1)(c): one of the following conditions is met as of the member's retirement date:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-17-401(1)(c)(i): the member has accrued at least six years of service credit and has attained an age of 70 years;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-17-401(1)(c)(ii): the member has accrued at least 10 years of service credit and has attained an age of 62 years;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-17-401(1)(c)(iii): the member has accrued at least 20 years of service credit and has attained an age of 55 years; or
Utah Code Annotated § 49-17-401(1)(c)(iv): the member has accrued at least 25 years of service credit.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-17-401(2): (2)(a)(i)
Utah Code Annotated § 49-17-401(2)(a): The member's retirement date:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-17-401(2)(a)(i): shall be the 1st or the 16th day of the month, as selected by the member;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-17-401(2)(a)(ii): shall be on or after the date of termination; and
Utah Code Annotated § 49-17-401(2)(a)(iii): may not be more than 90 days before or after the date the application is received by the office.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-17-401(2)(b): (2)(a)(i) A member may not be employed by a participating employer in the system established by this chapter on the retirement date selected under Subsection


Utah Code Annotated § 49-17-402 Calculation of retirement allowance.
--------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-17-402(1): A retiree under this system shall receive an allowance equal to:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-17-402(1)(a): 5% of the final average monthly salary multiplied by the number of years of service credit, limited to 10 years; plus
Utah Code Annotated § 49-17-402(1)(b): 2.25% of the final average monthly salary multiplied by the number of years of service credit in excess of 10 years and up to and including 20 years; plus
Utah Code Annotated § 49-17-402(1)(c): 1% of the final average monthly salary multiplied by the number of years of service credit in excess of 20 years.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-17-402(2): (2)(b); (2)(a)
Utah Code Annotated § 49-17-402(2)(a): (2)(b) Except as modified by cost-of-living adjustments and except as provided under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 49-17-402(2)(b): (2)(a) The allowance limitation under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 49-17-402(3): If the retiree has attained the age of 55 years and has 20 years or more but less than 25 years of service credit, the retiree shall receive an early retirement reduction to the allowance based on an actuarial calculation assuming a normal retirement age of 65 years.


Utah Code Annotated § 49-17-403 Minimum allowance.
--------------------------------------------------
Beginning July 1, 1990, all retirees or beneficiaries under this chapter who receive an allowance less than $1,000 per month shall have the allowance increased 10%, but the increased allowance may not equal more than $1,000.

Utah Code Annotated § 49-17-405 Annual cost-of-living adjustment.
-----------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-17-405(1): 49-17-402; Part 5, Death Benefit The office shall make an annual cost-of-living adjustment to:

Utah Code Annotated § 49-17-405(2):

Utah Code Annotated - Title 49 - Chapter 18 - Judges' Noncontributory Retirement Act
************************************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-101 Title.
--------------------------------------
This chapter is known as the "Judges' Noncontributory Retirement Act."

Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-102 Definitions.
--------------------------------------------
As used in this chapter:Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-102(1): 
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-102(1)(a): "Compensation" means the total amount of payments which are currently includable in gross income made by a participating employer to a member of this system for services rendered to the participating employer.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-102(1)(b): "Compensation" includes:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-102(1)(b)(i): performance-based bonuses;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-102(1)(b)(ii): cost-of-living adjustments;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-102(1)(b)(iii): payments subject to Social Security deductions;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-102(1)(b)(iv): any payments in excess of the maximum amount subject to deduction under Social Security law; and
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-102(1)(b)(v): amounts which the member authorizes to be deducted or reduced for salary deferral or other benefits authorized by federal law.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-102(1)(c): "Compensation" for purposes of this chapter may not exceed the amount allowed under Internal Revenue Code Section 401(a)(17).
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-102(1)(d): "Compensation" does not include:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-102(1)(d)(i): the monetary value of remuneration paid in kind, such as a residence or use of equipment;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-102(1)(d)(ii): all contributions made by a participating employer under a system or plan for the benefit of a member or participant;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-102(1)(d)(iii): salary paid to a temporary or exempt employee;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-102(1)(d)(iv): payments upon termination or any other special payments including early retirement inducements; or
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-102(1)(d)(v): uniform, travel, or similar payments.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-102(2): (2)(a); (b); (c); (2)(b); (2)(a) "Final average salary" means the amount calculated by averaging the highest two years of annual compensation preceding retirement, subject to Subsections
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-102(2)(a): (2)(b) Except as provided in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-102(2)(b): (2)(a) In cases where the participating employer provides acceptable documentation to the board, the limitation in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-102(2)(b)(i): the member has transferred from another agency; or
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-102(2)(b)(ii): the member has been promoted to a new position.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-102(2)(c): The annual compensation used to calculate final average salary shall be based on the state's fiscal year.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-102(3): 78A-1-101 "Judge" means a judge or justice of the courts of record as enumerated in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-102(4): "Participating employer" means the state.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-102(5): "System" means the Judges' Noncontributory Retirement System created under this chapter.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-102(6): "Years of service credit" means the number of periods, each to consist of 12 full months or as determined by the board, whether consecutive or not, during which a judge was employed by a participating employer.


Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-103 Creation of system.

There is created for judges the "Judges' Noncontributory Retirement System."

Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-104 Creation of trust fund.
-------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-104(1): There is created the "Judges' Noncontributory Retirement Trust Fund" for the purpose of paying the benefits and costs of administering this system.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-104(2): The fund shall consist of all money, including interest, and assets transferred to it under any terminated system, the money paid into it under this system, whether in the form of cash, securities, or other assets, and of all money received from any other source.

Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-401 Eligibility for an allowance -- Date of retirement -- Qualifications.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-401(1): A member is qualified to receive an allowance when:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-401(1)(a): the member ceases actual work for every participating employer that employs the member before the member's retirement date and provides evidence of the termination;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-401(1)(b): the member has submitted to the office a retirement application form that states the member's proposed retirement date; and
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-401(1)(c): one of the following conditions is met as of the member's retirement date:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-401(1)(c)(i): the member has accrued at least six years of service credit and has attained an age of 70 years;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-401(1)(c)(ii): the member has accrued at least 10 years of service credit and has attained an age of 62 years;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-401(1)(c)(iii): the member has accrued at least 20 years of service credit and has attained an age of 55 years; or
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-401(1)(c)(iv): the member has accrued at least 25 years of service credit.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-401(2): (2)(a)(i)
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-401(2)(a): The member's retirement date:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-401(2)(a)(i): shall be the 1st or the 16th day of the month, as selected by the member;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-401(2)(a)(ii): shall be on or after the date of termination; and
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-401(2)(a)(iii): may not be more than 90 days before or after the date the application is received by the office.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-401(2)(b): (2)(a)(i) A member may not be employed by a participating employer in the system established by this chapter on the retirement date selected under Subsection


Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-402 Calculation of retirement allowance.
--------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-402(1): A retiree under this system shall receive an allowance equal to:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-402(1)(a): 5% of the final average monthly salary multiplied by the number of years of service credit, limited to 10 years; plus
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-402(1)(b): 2.25% of the final average monthly salary multiplied by the number of years of service credit in excess of 10 years and up to and including 20 years; plus
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-402(1)(c): 1% of the final average monthly salary multiplied by the number of years of service credit in excess of 20 years.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-402(2): (2)(b); (2)(a)
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-402(2)(a): (2)(b) Except as modified by cost-of-living adjustments and except as provided under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-402(2)(b): (2)(a) The allowance limitation under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-402(3): If the retiree has attained the age of 55 years and has 20 years or more but less than 25 years of service credit, the retiree shall receive an early retirement reduction to the allowance based on an actuarial calculation assuming a normal retirement age of 65 years.


Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-403 Annual cost-of-living adjustment.
-----------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-403(1): 49-18-402; Part 5, Death Benefit The office shall make an annual cost-of-living adjustment to:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-403(1)(a): 49-18-402; Part 5, Death Benefit an allowance paid under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-403(1)(b): a payment made to an alternate payee under a domestic relations order, if the payment is to be paid as a percentage of the allowance rather than a specific dollar amount.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-403(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-403(2)(a): The allowance shall be increased by the annual increase in the Consumer Price Index up to a maximum of 4%.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-403(2)(b): Annual increases in the Consumer Price Index in excess of 4% shall be accumulated and used in subsequent adjustments when the increase in the Consumer Price Index is less than 4%.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-403(3): The Consumer Price Index used in calculating adjustments shall be a United States Bureau of Labor Statistics Consumer Price Index average as determined by the board.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-403(4): The cost-of-living adjustment made under this section may not decrease the allowance.


Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-501 Death benefit for members before retirement -- Computation.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-501(1): 49-18-402 Upon the receipt of acceptable proof of death of a member before the member's retirement date, the member's surviving spouse shall have the choice of the following death benefits:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-501(1)(a): a refund of the member's member contributions, if any, plus 65% of the member's most recent 12 months' compensation prior to death; or
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-501(1)(b): 49-18-402 an allowance equal to 65% of the allowance computed in accordance with Section
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-501(2): 49-11-609; 49-11-610 If there is no surviving spouse, member contributions shall be refunded to a beneficiary, in accordance with Sections
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-501(3): 
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-501(3)(a): A surviving spouse who requests a benefit under this section shall apply in writing to the office.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-501(3)(b): The allowance shall begin on the first day of the month:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-501(3)(b)(i): following the month in which the member died, if the application is received by the office within 90 days of the member's death; or
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-501(3)(b)(ii): following the month in which the application is received by the office, if the application is received by the office more than 90 days after the member's death.

------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-502(1): The death benefit payable to a retiree's surviving spouse is an allowance equal to 65% of the allowance which was being paid to the retiree at the time of death.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-502(2): (1); 49-18-402; (2)(a)

Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-502(3)(b)(i): member or participant died, if the application is received by the office within 90 days of the date of death of the member or participant; or
Utah Code Annotated § 49-18-502(3)(b)(ii): application is received by the office, if the application is received by the office more than 90 days after the date of death of the member or participant.

Utah Code Annotated - Title 49 - Chapter 19 - Utah Governors' and Legislators' Retirement Act
*********************************************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-101 Title.
--------------------------------------
This chapter is known as the "Utah Governors' and Legislators' Retirement Act."

Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-102 Definitions.
--------------------------------------------
As used in this chapter:Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-102(1): "Governor" includes former governors.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-102(2): "Legislator" includes former legislators.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-102(3): "Plan" means the Utah Governors' and Legislators' Retirement Plan created under this chapter.


Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-103 Creation of plan.
-------------------------------------------------
There is created for Utah governors and legislators the "Utah Governors' and Legislators' Retirement Plan."

Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-104 Creation of trust fund.
-------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-104(1): There is created the "Utah Governors' and Legislators' Retirement Trust Fund" for the purpose of paying the benefits and costs of administering this plan.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-104(2): The fund shall consist of all money paid into it, including interest, in accordance with this chapter, whether in the form of cash, securities, or other assets, and of all money received from any other source.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-104(3): Chapter 11, Utah State Retirement Systems Administration Custody, management, and investment of the fund shall be governed by


Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-201 Plan participation -- Eligibility.
------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-201(1): A governor or legislator is eligible for service credit in this plan during their term of service in their elected position if the governor or legislator:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-201(1)(a): entered office before July 1, 2011; or
Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-201(1)(b): accrued service credit in a Tier I system or plan administered by the board before July 1, 2011.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-201(2): Chapter 22, Part 4, Tier II Defined Contribution Plan; Chapter 22, Part 3, Tier II Hybrid Retirement System A governor or legislator initially entering office on or after July 1, 2011, who does not have service credit accrued before July 1, 2011, in a Tier I system or plan administered by the board:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-201(2)(a): may not participate in this system;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-201(2)(b): Chapter 22, Part 4, Tier II Defined Contribution Plan is only eligible to participate in the Tier II Defined Contribution Plan established under
Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-201(2)(c): Chapter 22, Part 3, Tier II Hybrid Retirement System is not eligible to participate in the Tier II hybrid retirement system established under


Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-301 Contribution rate -- Annual legislative appropriation.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-301(1): The Legislature, by means of annual appropriations, shall maintain this plan on a financially and actuarially sound basis.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-301(2): The Legislature shall cause the appropriate amount to be paid to the office.


Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-401 Eligibility for an allowance -- Governor -- Legislator.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-401(1): A governor is qualified to receive an allowance when:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-401(1)(a): the governor has submitted to the office a retirement application form that states the proposed retirement date; and
Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-401(1)(b): one of the following conditions is met as of the retirement date:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-401(1)(b)(i): the governor has completed at least one full term in office and has attained an age of 65 years; or
Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-401(1)(b)(ii): the governor has served as governor of the state for at least 10 years and has attained an age of 62 years.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-401(2): A legislator is qualified to receive an allowance when:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-401(2)(a): the legislator has submitted to the office a retirement application form that states the proposed retirement date; and
Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-401(2)(b): one of the following conditions is met as of the retirement date:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-401(2)(b)(i): the legislator has completed at least four years in the Legislature and has attained an age of 65 years; or
Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-401(2)(b)(ii): the legislator has completed at least 10 years in the Legislature and has attained an age of 62 years.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-401(3): 
Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-401(3)(a): The retirement date shall be the 1st or the 16th day of the month as selected by the member.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-401(3)(b): The retirement date may not be more than 90 days before or after the date the application is received by the office.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-401(4): A member who withdraws member contributions shall forfeit all allowances based on those contributions.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-401(5): If a retired legislator is elected to another term in the Legislature or continues to serve in the Legislature, the legislative allowance ceases at the beginning of each session under rules established by the board, but is restored at the same amount at the end of the session.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-401(6): A member receiving an allowance while serving as a legislator is eligible for additional service credits and allowance adjustments at the end of each term of office if the legislator continues as a contributing member during the member's service as a legislator.


Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-402 Calculation of allowance -- Reduction for early retirement.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-402(1): 49-19-404
Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-402(1)(a): 49-19-404 The base retirement amount for a governor under this plan is $500 per term, adjusted as provided in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-402(1)(b): A governor's allowance shall be calculated by multiplying the base retirement amount at the retirement date by the number of terms the governor served, including fractions of terms.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-402(2): 49-19-404
Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-402(2)(a): 49-19-404 The base retirement amount for a legislator under this plan is $10 per year of service in the Legislature, adjusted as provided in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-402(2)(b): A legislator's allowance shall be calculated by multiplying the base retirement amount at the retirement date by the number of years the legislator served, including fractions of years.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-402(3): If a governor or legislator retires prior to age 65, the allowance shall be reduced by 3% for each year of retirement between age 62 and age 65.

Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-403(1): Title 67, Chapter 22, State Officer Compensation; 49-11-801 A governor or legislator may elect to forfeit the allowance provided by this chapter and in lieu thereof participate, on the same basis as other state elected and appointed officers under

Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-403(2)(b): is subject to requirements under federal law and rules made by the board.


Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-404 Annual cost-of-living adjustment.
-----------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-404(1): 49-19-402; Part 5, Death Benefit; 49-19-402 The office shall make an annual cost-of-living adjustment to:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-404(1)(a): 49-19-402; Part 5, Death Benefit an original allowance paid under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-404(1)(b): an original payment made to an alternate payee under a domestic relations order, if the payment is to be paid as a percentage of the allowance rather than a specific dollar amount; and
Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-404(1)(c): 49-19-402 the base retirement amount for governors and legislators under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-404(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-404(2)(a): The original allowance shall be increased by the annual increase in the Consumer Price Index up to a maximum of 4%.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-404(2)(b): Annual increases in the Consumer Price Index in excess of 4% shall be accumulated and used in subsequent adjustments when the increase in the Consumer Price Index is less than 4%.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-404(3): The Consumer Price Index used in calculating adjustments shall be a United States Bureau of Labor Statistics Consumer Price Index average as determined by the board.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-404(4): The cost-of-living adjustment made under this section may not decrease the allowance.


Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-501 Death of member or retiree -- Surviving spouse benefit.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-501(1): Upon the death of a governor or legislator who has not yet retired and who has completed four or more years in the elected office, the member's surviving spouse shall receive an allowance equal to 50% of the allowance to which the governor or legislator would have been entitled upon reaching age 65, if the governor or legislator and surviving spouse had been married at least six months.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-501(2): Upon the death of a governor or legislator receiving an allowance under this plan, the member's surviving spouse is entitled to an allowance equal to 50% of the allowance being paid to the member at the time of death.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-501(3): 
Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-501(3)(a): A surviving spouse who requests a benefit under this section shall apply in writing to the office.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-501(3)(b): The allowance shall begin on the first day of the month:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-501(3)(b)(i): following the month in which the member died, if the application is received by the office within 90 days of the member's death; or
Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-501(3)(b)(ii): following the month in which the application is received by the office, if the application is received by the office more than 90 days after the member's death.


Utah Code Annotated § 49-19-502 Surviving spouse at the time of death includes certain former spouses -- Benefit calculation for former spouse.

Utah Code Annotated - Title 49 - Chapter 20 - Public Employees' Benefit and Insurance Program Act
*************************************************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-101 Title.
--------------------------------------
This chapter is known as the "Public Employees' Benefit and Insurance Program Act."

Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-102 Definitions.
--------------------------------------------
As used in this chapter:Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-102(1): "Covered employer" means an employer that offers employee benefit plans under this chapter to its employees and their dependents.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-102(2): "Covered individual" means an employee and the employee's dependents eligible for coverage under this chapter.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-102(3): "Employee Benefit Plans" means any group health, dental, medical, disability, life insurance, medicare supplement, conversion coverage, cafeteria, flex plans, or other program for covered individuals administered by the Public Employees' Benefit and Insurance Program.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-102(4): "Employer" means the state, its political subdivisions, and educational institutions.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-102(5): "Program" means the Public Employees' Benefit and Insurance Program.


Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-103 Creation of insurance program.
--------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-103(1): There is created for the employees of the state, its educational institutions, and political subdivisions the "Public Employees' Benefit and Insurance Program" within the office.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-103(2): The program may also be known and function as the Public Employees' Health Program, PEHP, or PEHP Health and Benefits.


Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-104 Creation of fund.
-------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-104(1): There is created the "Public Employees' Trust Fund" for the purpose of paying the benefits and the costs of administering this program.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-104(2): The fund shall consist of all money and interest paid into it in accordance with this chapter, whether in the form of cash, securities, or other assets, and of all money received from any other source.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-104(3): Chapter 11, Utah State Retirement Systems Administration Custody, management, and investment of the fund shall be governed by


Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-105 Purpose -- Benefits are not a continuing obligation.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-105(1): The purpose of this chapter is to provide a mechanism for covered employers to provide covered individuals with group health, dental, medical, disability, life insurance, medicare supplement, conversion coverage, cafeteria, flex plan, and other programs requested by the state, its political subdivisions, or educational institutions in the most efficient and economical manner.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-105(2): The benefits provided to a covered individual under this chapter do not constitute a continuing obligation of the state, its political subdivisions, or educational institutions.


Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-201 Program participation -- Eligibility -- Optional for certain groups.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-201(1): 
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-201(1)(a): The state shall participate in the program on behalf of the state's employees.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-201(1)(b): Other employers, including political subdivisions and educational institutions, are eligible, but are not required, to participate in the program on behalf of their employees.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-201(2): 26B-3-908
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-201(2)(a): 26B-3-908 As provided in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-201(2)(b): If the Department of Health and Human Services participates in the program under the provisions of this Subsection (2), all insurance risk associated with the Utah Children's Health Insurance Program shall be the responsibility of the Department of Health and Human Services and not the program or the office.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-201(3): 53-2d-703 Volunteer emergency medical service personnel are eligible to participate in the program in accordance with Section
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-201(4): A covered individual shall be eligible for coverage after termination of employment under rules adopted by the board.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-201(5): Only the following are eligible for Medicare supplement coverage under this chapter upon becoming eligible for Medicare Part A and Part B coverage:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-201(5)(a): retirees;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-201(5)(b): members;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-201(5)(c): participants;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-201(5)(d): employees who have medical employee benefit plan coverage at the time of their retirement; and
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-201(5)(e): current spouses of those who are eligible under Subsections (5)(a) through (d).

Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-301 Payments made by employer and employee.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------
The program shall be maintained on a financially and actuarially sound basis by payments from covered employers and covered individuals.

Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-401 Program -- Powers and duties.
-------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-401(1): (1)(a); (b); (e); (h); Title 26B, Chapter 3, Part 9, Utah Children's Health Insurance Program; 49-20-202(1)(a); 26B-8-411; 63G-6a-103; Title 26B, Utah Health and Human Services Code The program shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-401(1)(a): act as a self-insurer of employee benefit plans and administer those plans;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-401(1)(b): enter into contracts with private insurers or carriers to underwrite employee benefit plans as considered appropriate by the program;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-401(1)(c): indemnify employee benefit plans or purchase commercial reinsurance as considered appropriate by the program;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-401(1)(d): provide descriptions of all employee benefit plans under this chapter in cooperation with covered employers;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-401(1)(e): process claims for all employee benefit plans under this chapter or enter into contracts, after competitive bids are taken, with other benefit administrators to provide for the administration of the claims process;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-401(1)(f): obtain an annual actuarial review of all health and dental benefit plans and a periodic review of all other employee benefit plans;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-401(1)(g): consult with the covered employers to evaluate employee benefit plans and develop recommendations for benefit changes;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-401(1)(h): annually submit a budget and audited financial statements to the governor and Legislature that includes total projected benefit costs and administrative costs;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-401(1)(i): maintain reserves sufficient to liquidate the unrevealed claims liability and other liabilities of the employee benefit plans as certified by the program's consulting actuary;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-401(1)(j): submit, in advance, the program's recommended benefit and rate adjustments for state employees, which may include actuarially substantiated member premium differentials between networks to:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-401(1)(j)(i): the Legislature; and
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-401(1)(j)(ii): the director of the state Division of Human Resource Management;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-401(1)(k): determine benefits and rates, upon approval of the board, for multi-employer risk pools, retiree coverage, and conversion coverage;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-401(1)(l): determine benefits and rates based on the total estimated costs and the employee premium share established by the Legislature, upon approval of the board, for state employees;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-401(1)(m): administer benefits and rates, upon ratification of the board, for single-employer risk pools;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-401(1)(n): request proposals for one or more out-of-state provider networks and a dental health plan administered by a third-party carrier at least once every three years for the purposes of:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-401(1)(n)(i): stimulating competition for the benefit of covered individuals;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-401(1)(n)(ii): establishing better geographical coverage of medical care services; and
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-401(1)(n)(iii): providing coverage for both active and retired covered individuals;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-401(1)(o): for a proposal that meets the criteria specified in a request for proposals and is accepted by the program:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-401(1)(o)(i): offer the proposal to active and retired state-covered individuals; and
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-401(1)(o)(ii): at the option of the covered employer, offer the proposal to active and retired covered individuals of other covered employers;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-401(1)(p): (1)(a); (b); (e); (h); Title 26B, Chapter 3, Part 9, Utah Children's Health Insurance Program perform the same functions established in Subsections
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-401(1)(q): establish rules and procedures governing the admission of political subdivisions or educational institutions and their employees to the program;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-401(1)(r): 49-20-202(1)(a)
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-401(1)(r)(i): contract directly with medical providers to provide services for covered individuals at commercially competitive rates; and
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-401(1)(r)(ii): 49-20-202(1)(a)

Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-401(1)(s): 26B-8-411

Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-402 Reserves to be held -- Refunds.
---------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-402(1): The reserves in a risk pool in a given fiscal year shall be maintained at the level recommended by the program's consulting actuary and approved or ratified by the board.  If the reserves drop below that level, covered employers in the risk pool are required to cure any deficiency in the reserve.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-402(2): If substantial excess reserves are accrued above those required by this chapter, and the board determines that a refund is appropriate, a refund shall be made:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-402(2)(a): to covered employers which shall then make a refund to covered individuals on the basis of the contribution of each to the plan; or
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-402(2)(b): directly to covered individuals on the basis of the contribution of each to the plan.


Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-403 Assistance to members in purchase of life, health, dental, and medical insurance after retirement -- Employment of personnel to administer section.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-403(1): The program may assist active and retired covered individuals and inactive covered individuals of the covered employers to purchase life, health, dental, and medical coverage on a group basis which can be continued after retirement under rules adopted by the board.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-403(2): The executive director may employ any personnel, including consultants, to administer this section.

Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-405 Audit required -- Report to governor and Legislature.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
The Insurance Department shall biennially audit the Public Employees' Trust Fund and programs authorized under this chapter and report its findings to the governor and the Legislature, but the commissioner may accept the annual audited statement of the programs under this chapter in lieu of the biennial audit requirement.

Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-417 Insurance coverage for amino acid-based formula.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-417(1): 31A-22-634(1); Title 58, Chapter 17b, Pharmacy Practice Act; Title 58, Chapter 67, Utah Medical Practice Act; Title 58, Chapter 68, Utah Osteopathic Medical Practice Act; (2) As used in this section:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-417(1)(a): "Amino acid-based elemental formula" means a nutrition formula:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-417(1)(a)(i): made from individual nonallergenic amino acids that are broken down to enhance absorption and digestion; and
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-417(1)(a)(ii): designed for individuals who have a dysfunctional or shortened gastrointestinal tract and are unable to tolerate and absorb whole foods or formulas composed of whole proteins, fats, or carbohydrates.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-417(1)(b): "Eosinophilic gastrointestinal disorder" means a disorder characterized by having above normal amounts of eosinophils in one or more specific places anywhere in the digestive system.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-417(1)(c): "Food protein-induced enterocolitis syndrome" means a disorder characterized by an  abnormal immune response to an ingested food, resulting in gastrointestinal inflammation.

Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-421 Prescription discount program.
--------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-421(1): 26B-4-401; 58-17b-102; 31A-46-102 As used in this section:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-421(1)(a): "Discount program" means the prescription discount program created by this section.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-421(1)(b): 26B-4-401 "Epinephrine auto-injector" means the same as that term is defined in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-421(1)(c): "Insulin" means a prescription drug that contains insulin.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-421(1)(d): "Participant" means a resident of Utah who:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-421(1)(d)(i): has a prescription or standing prescription for a qualified prescription;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-421(1)(d)(ii): does not receive health coverage under the program; and
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-421(1)(d)(iii): enrolls in the discount program.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-421(1)(e): 58-17b-102 "Prescription drug" means the same as that term is defined in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-421(1)(f): "Qualified prescription" means a prescription drug, including insulin and epinephrine auto-injectors, that the program has determined:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-421(1)(f)(i): treats a serious, prevalent, and ongoing condition;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-421(1)(f)(ii): does not have a generic substitute;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-421(1)(f)(iii): qualifies for a substantial rebate; and
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-421(1)(f)(iv): would not result in financial losses to the state risk pool if sold as part of the discount program.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-421(1)(g): 31A-46-102 "Rebate" means the same as that term is defined in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-421(2): The program shall create a prescription discount program for a participant to purchase a qualified prescription at a discounted, post-rebate price.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-421(3): The program shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-421(3)(a): provide a participant with a card or electronic document that identifies the participant as eligible for the discount on a qualified prescription;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-421(3)(b): provide a participant with information about pharmacies that will honor the discount; and
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-421(3)(c): provide a participant with instructions to pursue a reimbursement of the purchase price from the participant's health insurer.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-421(4): The program may not retain any amount of a rebate for a qualified prescription except for an amount necessary to make the state risk pool whole for providing the qualified prescription to participants.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-421(5): For each drug added to the discount program, the program shall notify the Health and Human Services Interim Committee, providing:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-421(5)(a): the name of the drug; and
Utah Code Annotated § 49-20-421(5)(b): the primary condition the drug treats.

Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-101 Title.
--------------------------------------
This chapter is known as the "Public Employees' Long-Term Disability Act."

Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-102 Definitions.
--------------------------------------------
As used in this chapter:Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-102(1): "Date of disability" means the date on which a period of total disability begins, and may not begin on or before the last day of performing full-duty work in the eligible employee's regular occupation.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-102(2): 49-12-102; 49-13-102; 49-22-102; 49-14-102; 49-15-102; 49-23-102; 49-23-102; 49-17-102; 49-18-102; 49-12-203(4); 49-13-203(4); 49-14-203(1); 49-15-203(1); 49-21-201
