Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-102(2)(a)(iii): an employee who is covered by a retirement program offered by a public or private system, organization, or company designated by the Utah Board of Higher Education.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-102(2)(b): 49-21-201 "Eligible employee" does not include:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-102(2)(b)(i): 49-21-201 any employee that is exempt from coverage under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-102(2)(b)(ii): a retiree.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-102(3): "Elimination period" means the three months at the beginning of each continuous period of total disability for which no benefit will be paid.  The elimination period begins on the nearest first day of the month from the date of disability.  The elimination period may include a one-time trial return to work period of less than 15 consecutive calendar days.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-102(4): 
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-102(4)(a): "Gainful employment" means any occupation or employment position in the state that:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-102(4)(a)(i): contemplates continued employment during a fiscal or calendar year; and
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-102(4)(a)(ii): would pay an amount equal to or greater than 40 hours per week at the legally required minimum wage, regardless of the number of hours worked.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-102(4)(b): "Gainful employment" does not mean that an occupation or employment position in the state is:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-102(4)(b)(i): available within any geographic boundaries of the state;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-102(4)(b)(ii): offered at a certain level of wages;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-102(4)(b)(iii): available at a particular number of hours per week; or
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-102(4)(b)(iv): currently available.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-102(5): 49-21-403 "Maximum benefit period" means the maximum period of time the monthly disability income benefit will be paid under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-102(6): 49-21-401 "Monthly disability benefit" means the monthly payments and accrual of service credit under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-102(7): "Objective medical impairment" means an impairment resulting from an injury or illness that is diagnosed by a physician and that is based on accepted objective medical tests or findings rather than subjective complaints.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-102(8): 49-21-401(9) "Ongoing disability" means, after the elimination period and the first 24 months of disability benefits, the complete inability due to objective medical impairment, as determined under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-102(9): "Own occupation disability" means the complete inability, due to objective medical impairment, whether physical or mental, to engage in the eligible employee's regular occupation during the elimination period and the first 24 months of disability benefits.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-102(10): "Physician" means a licensed physician.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-102(11): "Pilot period" means the period beginning on July 1, 2023, and ending on June 30, 2026.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-102(12): "Regular monthly salary" means the amount certified by the participating employer as the monthly salary of the eligible employee, unless there is a discrepancy between the certified amount and the amount actually paid, in which case the office shall determine the regular monthly salary.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-102(13): "Regular occupation" means either:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-102(13)(a): the primary duties performed by the eligible employee for the 12 months preceding the date of disability; or
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-102(13)(b): a permanent assignment of duty to the eligible employee, as long as the eligible employee has actually performed all the required duties of the permanent assignment of duty.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-102(14): "Rehabilitative employment" means any occupation or employment for wage or profit, for which the eligible employee is reasonably qualified to perform based on education, training, or experience.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-102(15): "Total disability" means:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-102(15)(a): own occupation disability; or
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-102(15)(b): ongoing disability.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-102(16): Title 34A, Chapter 2, Part 4, Compensation and Benefits
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-102(16)(a): Title 34A, Chapter 2, Part 4, Compensation and Benefits "Workers' compensation indemnity benefits" means benefits provided that are designed to replace wages under
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-102(16)(b): "Workers' compensation indemnity benefits" includes a settlement amount following a claim for indemnity benefits.


Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-103 Creation of program.
----------------------------------------------------
There is created for eligible employees the "Public Employees' Long-Term Disability Program."

Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-104 Creation of trust fund.
-------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-104(1): There is created the "Public Employees' Long-Term Disability Trust Fund" for the purpose of paying the benefits and costs of administering this program.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-104(2): The fund shall consist of all money and interest paid into it in accordance with this chapter, whether in the form of cash, securities, or other assets, and of all money received from any other source.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-104(3): Chapter 11, Utah State Retirement Systems Administration Custody, management, and investment of the fund shall be governed by

-------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-105(1): The purpose of this chapter is to provide long-term disability benefits for an eligible employee.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-105(2): 49-21-201; 49-20-102 Subject to the provisions of Section
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-105(3): The program shall be administered by the office, under policies and rules adopted by the board.

Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-301 Contributions to fund program -- Adjustment of premium rate.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-301(1): During each legislative session, the board shall certify to the Legislature the employer paid premium rate expressed as a percentage of salary which is required to fund the Public Employees' Long-Term Disability Trust Fund.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-301(2): Upon the board's recommendation, the Legislature shall adjust the premium rate to maintain adequate funding for the Public Employees' Long-Term Disability Trust Fund.


Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-401 Disability benefits -- Application -- Eligibility.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-401(1): An eligible employee shall apply for long-term disability benefits under this chapter by:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-401(1)(a): completing an application form prepared by the office;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-401(1)(b): signing a consent form allowing the office access to the eligible employee's medical records; and
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-401(1)(c): providing any documentation or information reasonably requested by the office.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-401(2): (2)(a)

Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-404 Annual adjustment to disability benefit.
------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-404(1): 
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-404(1)(a): An eligible employee receiving a monthly disability benefit shall receive an annual adjustment on the date following the end of the elimination period to reflect annual changes in the United States Bureau of Labor Statistics Consumer Price Index average as determined by the board.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-404(1)(b): This adjustment may not exceed adjustments made to retirees under the system which covered the eligible employee on the date of disability.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-404(2): If an employee is not participating in a system, the annual adjustment may not exceed the adjustment paid in the system which would cover the employee if the employee were participating in a system.


Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-405 Disability benefit -- Exclusions.
-----------------------------------------------------------------
A monthly disability benefit is not payable for the following:Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-405(1): self-inflicted injury;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-405(2): alcoholism;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-405(3): substance abuse;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-405(4): disability arising from or caused by acts of aggression committed by the eligible employee; or
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-405(5): the eligible employee committing or attempting to commit a felony or other illegal act.


Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-406 Rehabilitative employment -- Interview by disability specialist -- Maintaining eligibility -- Additional treatment and care.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-406(1): 
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-406(1)(a): If an eligible employee, during a period of total disability for which the monthly disability benefit is payable, engages in approved rehabilitative employment, the monthly disability benefit otherwise payable shall be reduced:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-406(1)(a)(i): by an amount equal to 50% of the income to which the eligible employee is entitled for the employment during the month; and
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-406(1)(a)(ii): so that the combined amount received from the rehabilitative employment and the monthly disability payment does not exceed 100% of the eligible employee's monthly salary prior to the employee's disability.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-406(1)(b): This rehabilitative benefit is payable for up to two years or to the end of the maximum benefit period, whichever occurs first.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-406(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-406(2)(a): The office shall review an eligible employee's total disability at least one time each year.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-406(2)(b): The office shall interview each eligible employee receiving a monthly disability benefit.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-406(2)(c): The office may refer the eligible employee to a rehabilitative or vocational specialist for a review of the eligible employee's condition and a written rehabilitation plan and return to work assistance.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-406(3): If an eligible employee receiving a monthly disability benefit fails to participate in an office-approved rehabilitation program within the limitations set forth by a physician or physician assistant, the monthly disability benefit may be reduced, suspended, or terminated.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-406(4): The office may, as a condition of paying a monthly disability benefit, require that the eligible employee receive medical care and treatment if that treatment is reasonable or usual according to current medical practices.


Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-408 Limitation of service credit accrual -- Disability benefits from a long-term disability program other than under this chapter.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Beginning on July 1, 2014, an eligible employee who receives a monthly disability benefit from a long-term disability program other than under this chapter and who is eligible for service credit under a system or plan shall accrue service credit in that system or plan until the earlier of:Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-408(1): the date of the eligible employee's death;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-408(2): the date the eligible employee retires from the system or plan; or
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-408(3): Title 49, Chapter 22, Part 4, Tier II Defined Contribution Plan; Title 49, Chapter 23, Part 4, Tier II Defined Contribution Plan the date the eligible employee has accumulated or would have accumulated service credit in a defined benefit system or plan under this title, sufficient to be eligible to retire with an unreduced allowance, if the employee had not:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-408(3)(a): Title 49, Chapter 22, Part 4, Tier II Defined Contribution Plan; Title 49, Chapter 23, Part 4, Tier II Defined Contribution Plan chosen a defined contribution plan under
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-408(3)(b): been a volunteer firefighter; or
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-408(3)(c): been exempted from a retirement system or plan under this title.


Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-409 Violations -- Penalties. 
---------------------------------------------------------
In addition to other remedies provided in this title, if an eligible employee knowingly makes a material misrepresentation to the program or knowingly fails to disclose the award or receipt of amounts to the program as required under SectionUtah Code Annotated § 49-21-409(1): suspend the monthly disability benefits to the eligible employee;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-409(2): terminate all monthly disability benefits to the eligible employee;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-409(3): terminate or cancel any other benefits provided under this title during a period of total disability; or
Utah Code Annotated § 49-21-409(4): require the eligible employee to repay the amount of any overpayment resulting from the violation to the program.


Utah Code Annotated - Title 49 - Chapter 22 - New Public Employees' Tier II Contributory Retirement Act
*******************************************************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-101 Title.
--------------------------------------
This chapter is known as the "New Public Employees' Tier II Contributory Retirement Act."

Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-102 Definitions.
--------------------------------------------
As used in this chapter:Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-102(1): 49-12-102 "Benefits normally provided" means the same as that term is defined in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-102(2): 53F-2-513; (2)
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-102(2)(a): "Compensation" means the total amount of payments made by a participating employer to a member of this system for services rendered to the participating employer, including:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-102(2)(a)(i): bonuses;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-102(2)(a)(ii): cost-of-living adjustments;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-102(2)(a)(iii): other payments currently includable in gross income and that are subject to social security deductions, including any payments in excess of the maximum amount subject to deduction under social security law;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-102(2)(a)(iv): amounts that the member authorizes to be deducted or reduced for salary deferral or other benefits authorized by federal law; and
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-102(2)(a)(v): member contributions.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-102(2)(b): "Compensation" for purposes of this chapter may not exceed the amount allowed under Internal Revenue Code, Section 401(a)(17).
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-102(2)(c): 53F-2-513 "Compensation" does not include:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-102(2)(c)(i): the monetary value of remuneration paid in kind, including a residence or use of equipment;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-102(2)(c)(ii): the cost of any employment benefits paid for by the participating employer;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-102(2)(c)(iii): compensation paid to a temporary employee or an employee otherwise ineligible for service credit;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-102(2)(c)(iv): any payments upon termination, including accumulated vacation, sick leave payments, severance payments, compensatory time payments, or any other special payments;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-102(2)(c)(v): any allowances or payments to a member for costs or expenses paid by the participating employer, including automobile costs, uniform costs, travel costs, tuition costs, housing costs, insurance costs, equipment costs, and dependent care costs; or
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-102(2)(c)(vi): 53F-2-513 a teacher salary bonus described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-102(2)(d): (2) The executive director may determine if a payment not listed under this Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-102(3): "Corresponding Tier I system" means the system or plan that would have covered the member if the member had initially entered employment before July 1, 2011.

Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-103 Creation of system.
---------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-103(1): There is created for members employed by a participating employer the "New Public Employees' Tier II Contributory Retirement System."
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-103(2): Part 3, Tier II Hybrid Retirement System; Part 4, Tier II Defined Contribution Plan The New Public Employees' Tier II Contributory Retirement System includes:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-103(2)(a): Part 3, Tier II Hybrid Retirement System the Tier II hybrid retirement system created in
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-103(2)(b): Part 4, Tier II Defined Contribution Plan the Tier II defined contribution plan created in
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-103(3): The system may also be known and function as the Public Employees' Tier 2 Contributory Retirement System, the Tier 2 Hybrid Retirement System, and the Tier 2 Defined Contribution Plan.


Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-104 Creation of trust fund.
-------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-104(1): There is created the "New Public Employees' Tier II Contributory Retirement Trust Fund" for the purpose of paying the benefits and costs of administering the defined benefit portion of this system.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-104(2): The fund shall consist of all money paid into it, including interest, in accordance with this chapter, whether in the form of cash, securities, or other assets, and of all money received from any other source.

Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-204 Higher education employees' eligibility requirements -- Election between different retirement plans -- Classification requirements -- Transfer between systems.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-204(1): 
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-204(1)(a): A regular full-time employee of an institution of higher education who is eligible to participate in either this system or in a retirement annuity contract with a public or private system, organization, or company, designated as described in Subsection (1)(c), shall, not later than January 1, 1979, elect to participate exclusively in this system or in an annuity contract allowed under this Subsection (1).
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-204(1)(b): The election is final, and no right exists to make any further election.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-204(1)(c): The Utah Board of Higher Education shall designate the public or private retirement systems, organizations, or companies that a regular full-time employee of an institution of higher education is eligible to participate in under Subsection (1)(a).
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-204(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-204(2)(a): A regular full-time employee hired by an institution of higher education after January 1, 1979, may participate only in the retirement plan designated for the person's employment classification.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-204(2)(b): Each institution of higher education shall prepare or amend existing employment classifications, under the direction of the Utah Board of Higher Education, so that each classification is assigned with either:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-204(2)(b)(i): this system; or
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-204(2)(b)(ii): a public or private system, organization, or company designated bythe Utah Board of Higher Education.

Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-204(2)(c)(i): has service credit in this system before the date of employment with the institution of higher education; and
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-204(2)(c)(ii): makes the election before participating in the system described in Subsection (2)(b)(ii).
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-204(3): A regular full-time employee hired by an institution of higher education on or after July 1, 2011, whose employment classification requires participation in this system may elect to continue participation in this system upon change to an employment classification that requires participation in a public or private system, organization, or company designated by:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-204(3)(a): except as provided in Subsection (3)(b), the Utah Board of Higher Education; or
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-204(3)(b): the technical college board of trustees of each technical college for regular full-time employees of each technical college.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-204(4): A regular full-time employee hired by an institution of higher education on or after July 1, 2011, whose employment classification requires participation in this system shall participate in this system.

Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-301 Contributions.
----------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-301(1): Participating employers and members shall pay the certified contribution rates to the office to maintain the defined benefit portion of this system on a financially and actuarially sound basis.

Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-305 Defined benefit service retirement plans -- Calculation of retirement allowance -- Social security limitations.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-305(1): (6)
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-305(1)(a): (6) Except as provided under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-305(1)(b): Options Two, Three, Four, Five, and Six are modifications of the Option One calculation.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-305(2): The Option One benefit is an annual allowance calculated as follows:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-305(2)(a): If the retiree is at least 65 years of age or has accrued at least 35 years of service credit, the allowance is an amount equal to 1.5% of the retiree's final average salary multiplied by the number of years of service credit accrued on and after July 1, 2011.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-305(2)(b): If the retiree is less than 65 years of age, the allowance shall be reduced by the full actuarial amount for each year of retirement from age 60 to age 65, unless the member has 35 or more years of accrued credit in which event no reduction is made to the allowance.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-305(2)(c): 
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-305(2)(c)(i): Years of service includes any fractions of years of service to which the retiree may be entitled.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-305(2)(c)(ii): At the time of retirement, if a retiree's combined years of actual, not purchased, service credit is within one-tenth of one year of the total years of service credit required for retirement, the retiree shall be considered to have the total years of service credit required for retirement.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-305(2)(d): An Option One allowance is only payable to the member during the member's lifetime.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-305(3): 49-11-609; 49-11-610 The allowance payable under Options Two, Three, Four, Five, and Six is calculated by reducing an Option One benefit based on actuarial computations to provide the following:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-305(3)(a): 49-11-609; 49-11-610 Option Two is a reduced allowance paid to and throughout the lifetime of the retiree, and, if the retiree receives less in annuity payments than the amount of the retiree's member contributions, the remaining balance of the retiree's member contributions shall be paid in accordance with Sections
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-305(3)(b): Option Three is a reduced allowance paid to and throughout the lifetime of the retiree, and, upon the death of the retiree, the same reduced allowance is paid to and throughout the lifetime of the retiree's lawful spouse at the time of retirement.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-305(3)(c): Option Four is a reduced allowance paid to and throughout the lifetime of the retiree, and upon the death of the retiree, an amount equal to one-half of the retiree's allowance is paid to and throughout the lifetime of the retiree's lawful spouse at the time of retirement.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-305(3)(d): Option Five is a modification of Option Three so that if the lawful spouse at the time of retirement predeceases the retiree, an allowance equivalent to the amount payable at the time of initial retirement under Option One shall be paid to the retiree for the remainder of the retiree's life, beginning on the first day of the month following the month in which the:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-305(3)(d)(i): spouse died, if notification and supporting documentation for the death are received by the office within 90 days of the spouse's death; or
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-305(3)(d)(ii): notification and supporting documentation for the death are received by the office, if the notification and supporting documentation are received by the office more than 90 days after the spouse's death.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-305(3)(e): Option Six is a modification of Option Four so that if the lawful spouse at the time of retirement predeceases the retiree, an allowance equivalent to the amount payable at the time of initial retirement under Option One shall be paid to the retiree for the remainder of the retiree's life, beginning on the first day of the month following the month in which the:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-305(3)(e)(i): spouse died, if notification and supporting documentation for the death are received by the office within 90 days of the spouse's death; or
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-305(3)(e)(ii): notification and supporting documentation for the death are received by the office, if the notification and supporting documentation are received by the office more than 90 days after the spouse's death.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-305(4): 
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-305(4)(a): If a retiree under Option One dies within 120 days after the retiree's retirement date, the retirement is canceled and the death shall be considered as that of a member before retirement.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-305(4)(b): Any payments made to the retiree shall be deducted from the amounts due to the beneficiary.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-305(5): (5)
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-305(5)(a): If a retiree retires under either Option Five or Six and subsequently divorces, the retiree may elect to convert the benefit to an Option One benefit at the time of divorce, if there is no court order filed in the matter.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-305(5)(b): (5) A conversion to an Option One benefit under this Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-305(6): A retiree may not choose payment of an allowance under a retirement option described in this section that is not applicable to that retiree, including because the retiree did not make member contributions or does not have a lawful spouse at the time of retirement.


Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-306 Allowance payable by lump-sum payment.
----------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-306(1): If a retiree's allowance, as computed under this chapter, amounts to $25 or less, the allowance may be settled by the office by making a lump-sum payment of an amount actuarially equivalent to the allowance.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-306(2): A payment made under this section constitutes a full and complete settlement of the retiree's claim against this system.

Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-308 Defined benefit annual cost-of-living adjustment.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-308(1): 49-22-305 The office shall make an annual cost-of-living adjustment to:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-308(1)(a): 49-22-305 an original allowance paid under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-308(1)(b): an original payment made to an alternate payee under a domestic relations order, if the payment is to be paid as a percentage of the allowance rather than a specific dollar amount.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-308(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-308(2)(a): The original allowance shall be increased by the annual increase in the Consumer Price Index up to a maximum of 2.5%.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-308(2)(b): Annual increases in the Consumer Price Index in excess of 2.5% shall be accumulated and used in subsequent adjustments when the annual increase in the Consumer Price Index is less than 2.5%.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-308(3): The Consumer Price Index used in calculating adjustments shall be a United States Bureau of Labor Statistics Consumer Price Index average as determined by the board.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-308(4): The cost-of-living adjustment made under this section may not decrease the allowance.


Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-309 Purchase of service credit -- Conditions -- Cost -- Nondiscrimination policy.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-309(1): 
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-309(1)(a): A member may purchase or a member and a participating employer may jointly purchase a maximum of five years of service credit which cannot otherwise be purchased under this title.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-309(1)(b): At a minimum, the years of service credit purchased shall be sufficient to allow the member to meet the retirement eligibility requirements of this system with no actuarial reduction.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-309(1)(c): The member's retirement date shall be immediately after the purchase of years of service credit.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-309(1)(d): The member shall pay at least 5% of the cost of the purchase.

Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-309(1)(e)(i): have at least five years of service credit; and
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-309(1)(e)(ii): otherwise meet federal eligibility requirements.

Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-309(3): Prior to making any purchase of years of service credit under this section, a participating employer shall adopt a purchase policy that includes nondiscriminatory participation standards for all regular full-time employees.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-309(4): Only members retiring from this system may purchase service credit under this section.

Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-502 Death of married members -- Service retirement benefits to surviving spouse.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-502(1): 49-22-305 As used in this section, "member's full allowance" means an Option Three allowance calculated under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-502(2): Upon the request of a deceased member's surviving spouse, the deceased member is considered to have retired under Option Three on the first day of the month following the month in which the member died if the following requirements are met:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-502(2)(a): the member has:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-502(2)(a)(i): 15 or more years of service credit;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-502(2)(a)(ii): attained age 62 with 10 or more years of service credit; or
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-502(2)(a)(iii): attained age 65 with four or more years of service credit; and
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-502(2)(b): the member dies leaving a surviving spouse.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-502(3): The surviving spouse who requests a benefit under this section shall apply in writing to the office.  The allowance shall begin on the first day of the month:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-502(3)(a): following the month in which the member died, if the application is received by the office within 90 days of the member's death; or
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-502(3)(b): following the month in which the application is received by the office, if the application is received by the office more than 90 days after the member's death.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-502(4): The allowance payable to a surviving spouse under Subsection (2) is as follows:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-502(4)(a): if the member has 25 or more years of service credit at the time of death, the surviving spouse shall receive the member's full allowance;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-502(4)(b): if the member has between 20-24 years of service credit and is not age 60 or older at the time of death, the surviving spouse shall receive 2/3 of the member's full allowance;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-502(4)(c): if the member has between 15-19 years of service credit and is not age 62 or older at the time of death, the surviving spouse shall receive 1/3 of the member's full allowance; or
Utah Code Annotated § 49-22-502(4)(d): if the member is age 60 or older with 20 or more years of service credit, age 62 or older with 10 or more years of service credit, or age 65 or older with four or more years of service credit at the time of death, the surviving spouse shall receive an Option Three benefit with actuarial reductions.

Utah Code Annotated - Title 49 - Chapter 23 - New Public Safety and Firefighter Tier II Contributory Retirement Act
*******************************************************************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-101 Title.
--------------------------------------
This chapter is known as the "New Public Safety and Firefighter Tier II Contributory Retirement Act."

Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-102 Definitions.
--------------------------------------------
As used in this chapter:Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-102(1): 
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-102(1)(a): "Compensation" means the total amount of payments that are includable in gross income received by a public safety service employee or a firefighter service employee as base income for the regularly scheduled work period.  The participating employer shall establish the regularly scheduled work period.  Base income shall be determined prior to the deduction of any amounts the public safety service employee or firefighter service employee authorizes to be deducted for salary deferral or other benefits authorized by federal law.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-102(1)(b): "Compensation" includes performance-based bonuses and cost-of-living adjustments.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-102(1)(c): "Compensation" does not include:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-102(1)(c)(i): overtime;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-102(1)(c)(ii): sick pay incentives;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-102(1)(c)(iii): retirement pay incentives;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-102(1)(c)(iv): the monetary value of remuneration paid in kind, as in a residence, use of equipment or uniform, travel, or similar payments;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-102(1)(c)(v): a lump-sum payment or special payment covering accumulated leave; and
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-102(1)(c)(vi): all contributions made by a participating employer under this system or under any other employee benefit system or plan maintained by a participating employer for the benefit of a member or participant.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-102(1)(d): "Compensation" for purposes of this chapter may not exceed the amount allowed under Section 401(a)(17), Internal Revenue Code.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-102(2): "Corresponding Tier I system" means the system or plan that would have covered the member if the member had initially entered employment before July 1, 2011.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-102(3): 53-6-102 "Dispatcher" means the same as that term is defined in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-102(4): 53-2d-402 "Emergency medical service personnel" means an individual who:

Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-102(4)(a)(iii): an emergency medical services technician;

Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-102(4)(c): has a primary job duty to provide emergency medical services as a first responder.

Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-103 Creation of system.
---------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-103(1): There is created for members employed by a participating employer the "New Public Safety and Firefighter Tier II Contributory Retirement System."
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-103(2): Part 3, Tier II Hybrid Retirement System; Part 4, Tier II Defined Contribution Plan The New Public Safety and Firefighter Tier II Contributory Retirement System includes:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-103(2)(a): Part 3, Tier II Hybrid Retirement System the Tier II hybrid retirement system created in
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-103(2)(b): Part 4, Tier II Defined Contribution Plan the Tier II defined contribution plan created in
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-103(3): The system may also be known and function as the Public Safety and Firefighter Tier 2 Contributory Retirement System, the Tier 2 Hybrid Retirement System, and the Tier 2 Defined Contribution Plan.


Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-104 Creation of trust fund.
-------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-104(1): There is created the "New Public Safety and Firefighter Tier II Contributory Retirement Trust Fund" for the purpose of paying the benefits and costs of administering the defined benefit portion of this system.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-104(2): The fund shall consist of all money paid into it, including interest, in accordance with this chapter, whether in the form of cash, securities, or other assets, and of all money received from any other source.

Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-202 Participation of employers -- Admission requirements.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-202(1): 49-15-202; 49-16-202
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-202(1)(a): An employer is a participating employer and may not withdraw from participation in this system.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-202(1)(b): 49-15-202; 49-16-202 A participating employer shall cover the participating employer's:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-202(1)(b)(i): 49-15-202 public safety service employees in accordance with Section
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-202(1)(b)(ii): 49-16-202 firefighter service employees in accordance with Section
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-202(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-202(2)(a): An employer may, by resolution of the employer's governing body, apply for admission to this system.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-202(2)(b): Upon approval of the resolution by the board, the employer is a participating employer in this system and is subject to this title.

Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-304 Defined benefit service retirement plans -- Calculation of retirement allowance -- Social security limitations.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-304(1): (6)
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-304(1)(a): (6) Except as provided under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-304(1)(b): Options Two, Three, Four, Five, and Six are modifications of the Option One calculation.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-304(2): The Option One benefit is an annual allowance calculated as follows:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-304(2)(a): If the retiree is at least 65 years of age or has accrued at least 25 years of service credit, the allowance is an amount equal to:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-304(2)(a)(i): 1.5% of the retiree's final average salary multiplied by the number of years of service credit accrued on and after July 1, 2011, but before July 1, 2020; plus
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-304(2)(a)(ii): 2% of the retiree's final average salary multiplied by the number of years of service credit accrued on and after July 1, 2020.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-304(2)(b): If the retiree is less than 65 years of age, the allowance shall be reduced by the full actuarial amount for each year of retirement from age 60 to age 65, unless the member has 25 or more years of accrued credit in which event no reduction is made to the allowance.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-304(2)(c): 
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-304(2)(c)(i): Years of service includes any fractions of years of service to which the retiree may be entitled.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-304(2)(c)(ii): At the time of retirement, if a retiree's combined years of actual, not purchased, service credit is within 1/10 of one year of the total years of service credit required for retirement, the retiree shall be considered to have the total years of service credit required for retirement.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-304(2)(d): An Option One allowance is only payable to the member during the member's lifetime.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-304(3): 49-11-609; 49-11-610 The allowance payable under Options Two, Three, Four, Five, and Six is calculated by reducing an Option One benefit based on actuarial computations to provide the following:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-304(3)(a): 49-11-609; 49-11-610 Option Two is a reduced allowance paid to and throughout the lifetime of the retiree, and, if the retiree receives less in annuity payments than the amount of the retiree's member contributions, the remaining balance of the retiree's member contributions shall be paid in accordance with Sections
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-304(3)(b): Option Three is a reduced allowance paid to and throughout the lifetime of the retiree, and, upon the death of the retiree, the same reduced allowance is paid to and throughout the lifetime of the retiree's lawful spouse at the time of retirement.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-304(3)(c): Option Four is a reduced allowance paid to and throughout the lifetime of the retiree, and upon the death of the retiree, an amount equal to 1/2 of the retiree's allowance is paid to and throughout the lifetime of the retiree's lawful spouse at the time of retirement.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-304(3)(d): Option Five is a modification of Option Three so that if the lawful spouse at the time of retirement predeceases the retiree, an allowance equivalent to the amount payable at the time of initial retirement under Option One shall be paid to the retiree for the remainder of the retiree's life, beginning on the first day of the month following the month in which the:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-304(3)(d)(i): spouse died, if notification and supporting documentation for the death are received by the office within 90 days of the spouse's death; or
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-304(3)(d)(ii): notification and supporting documentation for the death are received by the office, if the notification and supporting documentation are received by the office more than 90 days after the spouse's death.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-304(3)(e): Option Six is a modification of Option Four so that if the lawful spouse at the time of retirement predeceases the retiree, an allowance equivalent to the amount payable at the time of initial retirement under Option One shall be paid to the retiree for the remainder of the retiree's life, beginning on the first day of the month following the month in which the:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-304(3)(e)(i): spouse died, if notification and supporting documentation for the death are received by the office within 90 days of the spouse's death; or
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-304(3)(e)(ii): notification and supporting documentation for the death are received by the office, if the notification and supporting documentation are received by the office more than 90 days after the spouse's death.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-304(4): 
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-304(4)(a): If a retiree under Option One dies within 120 days after the retiree's retirement date, the retirement is canceled and the death shall be considered as that of a member before retirement.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-304(4)(b): Any payments made to the retiree shall be deducted from the amounts due to the beneficiary.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-304(5): (5)
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-304(5)(a): If a retiree retires under either Option Five or Six and subsequently divorces, the retiree may elect to convert the benefit to an Option One benefit at the time of divorce, if there is no court order filed in the matter.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-304(5)(b): (5) A conversion to an Option One benefit under this Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-304(6): A retiree may not choose payment of an allowance under a retirement option described in this section that is not applicable to that retiree, including because the retiree did not make member contributions or does not have a lawful spouse at the time of retirement.


Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-305 Allowance payable by lump-sum payment.
----------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-305(1): If a retiree's allowance, as computed under this chapter, amounts to $25 or less, the allowance may be settled by the office by making a lump-sum payment of an amount actuarially equivalent to the allowance.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-305(2): A payment made under this section constitutes a full and complete settlement of the retiree's claim against this system.


Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-306 Lump-sum death benefit for retiree and spouse.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-306(1): 
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-306(1)(a): Upon retirement, a retiree may elect to have the office deduct an actuarially determined amount from the retiree's allowance to provide a lump-sum benefit payable to a beneficiary upon the death of the retiree.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-306(1)(b): Upon retirement, a retiree may also elect to have an actuarially determined amount deducted from the retiree's allowance to provide a lump-sum death benefit payable to a beneficiary upon the death of the retiree's lawful spouse at the time of retirement.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-306(1)(c): The board may make rules for the administration of this lump-sum death benefit.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-306(2): 49-11-609; 49-11-610
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-306(2)(a): 49-11-609; 49-11-610 For a retiree who pays for a lump-sum death benefit under this section through a reduction of an allowance, benefits shall be paid in accordance with Sections
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-306(2)(b): If the retiree chooses Option Three, Four, Five, or Six, and a lump-sum death benefit is payable after the death of the retiree, the allowance shall be restored to its original amount.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-306(3): (3)
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-306(3)(a): A retiree may elect to cancel the lump-sum death benefit under this section.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-306(3)(b): (3) The cancellation under this Subsection

Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-307 Defined benefit annual cost-of-living adjustment.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-307(1): 49-23-305 The office shall make an annual cost-of-living adjustment to:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-307(1)(a): 49-23-305 an original allowance paid under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-307(1)(b): an original payment made to an alternate payee under a domestic relations order, if the payment is to be paid as a percentage of the allowance rather than a specific dollar amount.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-307(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-307(2)(a): The original allowance shall be increased by the annual increase in the Consumer Price Index up to a maximum of 2.5%.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-307(2)(b): Annual increases in the Consumer Price Index in excess of 2.5% shall be accumulated and used in subsequent adjustments when the annual increase in the Consumer Price Index is less than 2.5%.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-307(3): The Consumer Price Index used in calculating adjustments shall be a United States Bureau of Labor Statistics Consumer Price Index average as determined by the board.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-307(4): The cost-of-living adjustment made under this section may not decrease the allowance.


Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-308 Purchase of service credit -- Conditions -- Cost -- Nondiscrimination policy.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-308(1): 
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-308(1)(a): A member may purchase or a member and a participating employer may jointly purchase a maximum of five years of service credit which cannot otherwise be purchased under this title.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-308(1)(b): At a minimum, the years of service credit purchased shall be sufficient to allow the member to meet the retirement eligibility requirements of this system with no actuarial reduction.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-308(1)(c): The member's retirement date shall be immediately after the purchase of years of service credit.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-308(1)(d): The member shall pay at least 5% of the cost of the purchase.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-308(1)(e): To qualify for a purchase of service credit under this section, the member shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-308(1)(e)(i): have at least five years of service credit; and
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-308(1)(e)(ii): otherwise meet federal eligibility requirements.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-308(2): 49-11-403 The purchase price for the years of service credit shall be calculated and paid for as provided in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-308(3): Prior to making any purchase of years of service credit under this section, a participating employer shall adopt a purchase policy that includes nondiscriminatory participation standards for all regular full-time employees.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-308(4): Only members retiring from this system may purchase service credit under this section.

Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-502 Death of married members -- Service retirement benefits to surviving spouse.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-502(1): 49-23-304 As used in this section, "member's full allowance" means an Option Three allowance calculated under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-502(2): Upon the request of a deceased member's surviving spouse at the time of the member's death, the deceased member is considered to have retired under Option Three on the first day of the month following the month in which the member died if the following requirements are met:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-502(2)(a): the member has:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-502(2)(a)(i): 15 or more years of service credit;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-502(2)(a)(ii): attained age 62 with 10 or more years of service credit; or
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-502(2)(a)(iii): attained age 65 with four or more years of service credit; and
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-502(2)(b): the member dies leaving a surviving spouse.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-502(3): The surviving spouse who requests a benefit under this section shall apply in writing to the office. The allowance shall begin on the first day of the month:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-502(3)(a): following the month in which the member died, if the application is received by the office within 90 days of the member's death; or
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-502(3)(b): following the month in which the application is received by the office, if the application is received by the office more than 90 days after the member's death.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-502(4): The allowance payable to a surviving spouse under Subsection (2) is:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-502(4)(a): if the member has 25 or more years of service credit at the time of death, the surviving spouse shall receive the member's full allowance;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-502(4)(b): if the member has between 20-24 years of service credit and is not age 60 or older at the time of death, the surviving spouse shall receive two-thirds of the member's full allowance;
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-502(4)(c): if the member has between 15-19 years of service credit and is not age 62 or older at the time of death, the surviving spouse shall receive one-third of the member's full allowance; or
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-502(4)(d): if the member is age 60 or older with 20 or more years of service credit, age 62 or older with 10 or more years of service credit, or age 65 or older with four or more years of service credit at the time of death, the surviving spouse shall receive an Option Three benefit with actuarial reductions.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-502(5): 49-11-612 The benefit calculation for a surviving spouse with a valid domestic relations order benefits on file with the office before the member's death date in accordance with Section

Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-503(1)(a): If the member has accrued less than 20 years of public safety service or firefighter service credit, the surviving spouse shall receive:
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-503(1)(a)(i): a lump sum equal to six months of the active member's final average salary; and
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-503(1)(a)(ii): the greater of:

Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-503(1)(a)(ii)(B): an allowance equal to 2% of the member's final average monthly salary multiplied by the years of service credit accrued by the member.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-503(1)(b): 49-23-304 If the member has accrued 20 or more years of public safety service or firefighter service credit, the member shall be considered to have retired with an Option One allowance calculated without an actuarial reduction under Section

Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-503(2)(a): A volunteer firefighter is eligible for a line-of-duty death benefit under this section if the death results from external force, violence, or disease directly resulting from firefighter service.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-503(2)(b): The lowest monthly compensation of firefighters of a city of the first class in this state at the time of death shall be considered to be the final average monthly salary of a volunteer firefighter for purposes of computing these benefits.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-503(2)(c): 49-23-102(14) Each volunteer fire department shall maintain a current roll of all volunteer firefighters that meet the requirements of Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-503(3): 49-23-502; 49-23-502

Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-503(3)(b): 49-23-502 If the death is not classified as a line-of-duty death by the office, benefits are payable in accordance with Section
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-503(4): 
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-503(4)(a): A surviving spouse who qualifies for a monthly benefit under this section shall apply in writing to the office.
Utah Code Annotated § 49-23-503(4)(b): The allowance shall begin on the first day of the month following the month in which the:
